     â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     import os
     import cv2
     from ultralytics import YOLO
     
     # Load YOLO model once
     model = YOLO('best.pt')
     print("[INFO] Model loaded. Classes:", model.names)
     
     def process_frame(frame):
         results = model(frame)
         for result in results:
             for box in result.boxes:
                 x1, y1, x2, y2 = map(int, box.xyxy[0])
                 conf = box.conf[0].item()
                 cls = int(box.cls[0].item())
                 class_name = model.names.get(cls, f'Class {cls}')
                 label = f'{class_name} {conf:.2f}'
     
                 cv2.rectangle(frame, (x1, y1), (x2, y2), (0, 255, 0), 2)
                 (w, h), _ = cv2.getTextSize(label, cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 0.7, 2)
                 cv2.rectangle(frame, (x1, y1 - h - 5), (x1 + w, y1), (0, 255, 0), -1)
                 cv2.putText(frame, label, (x1, y1), cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX,
                             0.7, (0, 0, 0), 2, cv2.LINE_AA)
         return frame
     
     def process_images_in_directory(input_dir, output_dir):
         os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)
         supported_ext = ['.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.bmp']
     
         for filename in os.listdir(input_dir):
             if any(filename.lower().endswith(ext) for ext in supported_ext):
                 image_path = os.path.join(input_dir, filename)
                 frame = cv2.imread(image_path)
                 if frame is None:
                     print(f"[WARNING] Couldn't read {filename}, skipping.")
                     continue
     
                 processed_frame = process_frame(frame)
                 output_path = os.path.join(output_dir, filename)
                 cv2.imwrite(output_path, processed_frame)
                 print(f"[INFO] Processed and saved: {output_path}")
     
     if __name__ == '__main__':
         process_images_in_directory('input', 'static/predictions')
     â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

     from flask import Flask, render_template, request, jsonify, url_for, redirect, session
     from database_setup import Base, engine
     from dashboard import dashboard_bp
     from network_utils.status import status_bp
     from network import receive_sensor_data
     from AI_model import process_images_in_directory
     import os
     from network_utils.config_handler import load_config, save_config
     from network_utils.user_control import handle_manual_control
     from network_utils.auth import auth_bp
     # from datetime import timedelta  âŒ Remove if no longer using permanent sessions
     
     app = Flask(__name__)
     app.secret_key = "8e0b7a6e4fa24739b0a05c1e5dc889d1f6d49b91ce9b213ec2af3b110d9376b9s"
     # app.permanent_session_lifetime = timedelta(minutes=1)  âŒ Disable this to rely on browser session cookies
     
     Base.metadata.create_all(bind=engine)
     
     app.register_blueprint(auth_bp)
     app.register_blueprint(dashboard_bp)
     app.register_blueprint(status_bp)
     
     INPUT_DIR = 'input'
     OUTPUT_DIR = 'static/predictions'
     
     @app.route('/')
     def index():
         print("[DEBUG] Current session:", dict(session))  # Optional debugging
         if "user_id" not in session:
             return redirect(url_for("auth.login"))
         return render_template('index.html')
     
     @app.route('/run', methods=['POST'])
     def run_yolo():
         process_images_in_directory(INPUT_DIR, OUTPUT_DIR)
         return redirect(url_for('ai_model'))
     
     @app.route('/results')
     def ai_model():
         images = [
             f for f in os.listdir(OUTPUT_DIR)
             if f.lower().endswith(('.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.bmp'))
         ]
         return render_template('ai_model.html', images=images)
     
     @app.route('/receive', methods=['POST'])
     def receive_data():
         return receive_sensor_data(request)
     
     @app.route('/get_thresholds')
     def get_thresholds():
         return jsonify(load_config())
     
     @app.route('/set_thresholds', methods=['POST'])
     def set_thresholds():
         data = request.get_json()
         try:
             config = load_config()
             config["TEMP_THRESHOLD"] = int(data.get("temp_threshold", config["TEMP_THRESHOLD"]))
             config["HUM_THRESHOLD"] = int(data.get("hum_threshold", config["HUM_THRESHOLD"]))
             config["SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD"] = int(data.get("soil_moisture_threshold", config["SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD"]))
             save_config(config)
             print("[DEBUG] Thresholds updated:", config)
             return jsonify({"message": "Thresholds updated successfully."})
         except Exception as e:
             return jsonify({"message": f"Error: {str(e)}"}), 400
     
     @app.route("/manual-control", methods=["POST"])
     def manual_control():
         payload = request.get_json()
         result = handle_manual_control(payload)
         return jsonify(result), 200 if result.get("status") == "success" else 400
     
     
     @app.route('/about')
     def aboutus():
         return render_template("aboutus.html")
     
     @app.route("/logout")
     def logout():
         session.clear()
         return redirect(url_for("auth.login"))
     
     
     if __name__ == '__main__':
         app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=5000)

     from flask import Blueprint, render_template, jsonify
     from database_setup import SessionLocal, SensorData, KalmanFilterFusionData, WeightedAverageFusionData
     from collections import defaultdict
     import json
     
     dashboard_bp = Blueprint('dashboard', __name__)
     
     sensor_labels = {
         2001: "Temperature - DHT1 Internal",
         2002: "Humidity - DHT1 Internal",
         2003: "Temperature - DHT2 Internal",
         2004: "Humidity - DHT2 Internal",
         2005: "Soil Moisture - Plant 1",
         3001: "Temperature - DHT3 Internal",
         3002: "Humidity - DHT3 Internal",
         3003: "Temperature - DHT4 External",
         3004: "Humidity - DHT4 External",
         3005: "Soil Moisture - Plant 2"
     }
     
     @dashboard_bp.route("/dashboard")
     def dashboard():
         return render_template("dashboard.html")
     
     
     @dashboard_bp.route("/api/dashboard-data")
     def dashboard_data():
         session = SessionLocal()
         try:
             # --- RAW SENSOR DATA ---
             raw_data = session.query(SensorData).order_by(SensorData.Timestamp).limit(100).all()
             grouped_raw = defaultdict(list)
             for entry in raw_data:
                 grouped_raw[entry.SensorID].append({
                     "timestamp": entry.Timestamp.isoformat(),
                     "value": entry.Value
                 })
     
             raw_plot_data = [
                 {
                     "label": sensor_labels.get(sensor_id, f"Sensor {sensor_id}"),
                     "sensor_id": sensor_id,
                     "timestamps": [d["timestamp"] for d in data],
                     "values": [d["value"] for d in data]
                 }
                 for sensor_id, data in grouped_raw.items()
             ]
     
             # --- KALMAN FILTER FUSION DATA ---
             kalman_data = session.query(KalmanFilterFusionData).order_by(KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp).limit(100).all()
             grouped_kalman = defaultdict(list)
             for entry in kalman_data:
                 grouped_kalman[entry.SensorID].append({
                     "timestamp": entry.Timestamp.isoformat(),
                     "value": entry.FusedValue
                 })
             kalman_plot_data = [
                 {
                     "label": sensor_labels.get(sensor_id, f"Sensor {sensor_id}"),
                     "sensor_id": sensor_id,
                     "timestamps": [d["timestamp"] for d in data],
                     "values": [d["value"] for d in data]
                 }
                 for sensor_id, data in grouped_kalman.items()
             ]
     
             # --- WEIGHTED AVERAGE FUSION DATA ---
             weighted_data = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData).order_by(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp).limit(100).all()
             grouped_weighted = defaultdict(list)
             for entry in weighted_data:
                 grouped_weighted[entry.SensorType].append({
                     "timestamp": entry.Timestamp.isoformat(),
                     "value": entry.FusedValue
                 })
             weighted_plot_data = [
                 {
                     "sensor_type": sensor_type,
                     "timestamps": [d["timestamp"] for d in data],
                     "values": [d["value"] for d in data]
                 }
                 for sensor_type, data in grouped_weighted.items()
             ]
     
             return jsonify({
                 "raw": raw_plot_data,
                 "kalman": kalman_plot_data,
                 "weighted": weighted_plot_data
             })
     
         finally:
             session.close()
     â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

     â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker
     from database_setup import engine, Actuator, UserInteraction
     import pandas as pd
     
     # Create session
     Session = sessionmaker(bind=engine)
     session = Session()
     
     # === Fetch last row from Actuator table ===
     last_actuator = (
         session.query(Actuator)
         .order_by(Actuator.LastUpdated.desc())
         .first()
     )
     
     # Convert to dict
     actuator_data = {
         "ActuatorID": last_actuator.ActuatorID,
         "ActuatorName": last_actuator.ActuatorName,
         "Status": last_actuator.Status,
         "LastUpdated": last_actuator.LastUpdated,
         "UserID": last_actuator.UserID,
         "DeviceID": last_actuator.DeviceID
     } if last_actuator else {}
     
     # === Fetch last row from UserInteraction table ===
     last_interaction = (
         session.query(UserInteraction)
         .order_by(UserInteraction.Timestamp.desc())
         .first()
     )
     
     # Convert to dict
     interaction_data = {
         "InteractionID": last_interaction.InteractionID,
         "UserID": last_interaction.UserID,
         "DeviceID": last_interaction.DeviceID,
         "ActuatorID": last_interaction.ActuatorID,
         "Action": last_interaction.Action,
         "Timestamp": last_interaction.Timestamp
     } if last_interaction else {}
     
     # Close session
     session.close()
     
     # Print output
     print("\n=== Last Actuator Entry ===")
     print(pd.DataFrame([actuator_data]))
     
     print("\n=== Last UserInteraction Entry ===")
     print(pd.DataFrame([interaction_data]))

â”‚        import random
â”‚        from datetime import datetime, timedelta
â”‚        from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
â”‚        from faker import Faker
â”‚        from database_setup import (
â”‚            Base, engine, SessionLocal,
â”‚            UserCredentials, Device, Sensor,
â”‚            SensorData, KalmanFilterFusionData,
â”‚            Actuator
â”‚        )
â”‚        
â”‚        fake = Faker()
â”‚        
â”‚        # Use same sensor IDs from your fusion logic
â”‚        TEMP_SENSOR_IDS = [2099, 2092, 3093]
â”‚        HUM_SENSOR_IDS = [2091, 2034, 3027]
â”‚        ALL_SENSOR_IDS = TEMP_SENSOR_IDS + HUM_SENSOR_IDS
â”‚        
â”‚        def create_dummy_user(session: Session):
â”‚            user = UserCredentials(
â”‚                Username="test_user",
â”‚                PasswordHash="hashed_password",
â”‚                Email="test@example.com",
â”‚                FullName="Test User"
â”‚            )
â”‚            session.add(user)
â”‚            session.flush()  # get UserID for foreign keys
â”‚            return user
â”‚        
â”‚        def create_dummy_devices(session: Session):
â”‚            devices = []
â”‚            for i in range(1, 4):
â”‚                device = Device(
â”‚                    DeviceID=1000 + i,
â”‚                    DeviceName=f"Device_{i}",
â”‚                    Location=fake.city()
â”‚                )
â”‚                session.add(device)
â”‚                devices.append(device)
â”‚            session.flush()
â”‚            return devices
â”‚        
â”‚        def create_dummy_sensors(session: Session, devices):
â”‚            sensors = []
â”‚            sensor_definitions = [
â”‚                (TEMP_SENSOR_IDS[0], devices[0], "Temperature"),
â”‚                (TEMP_SENSOR_IDS[1], devices[1], "Temperature"),
â”‚                (TEMP_SENSOR_IDS[2], devices[2], "Temperature"),
â”‚                (HUM_SENSOR_IDS[0], devices[0], "Humidity"),
â”‚                (HUM_SENSOR_IDS[1], devices[1], "Humidity"),
â”‚                (HUM_SENSOR_IDS[2], devices[2], "Humidity"),
â”‚            ]
â”‚            for sensor_id, device, sensor_type in sensor_definitions:
â”‚                sensor = Sensor(
â”‚                    SensorID=sensor_id,
â”‚                    DeviceID=device.DeviceID,
â”‚                    SensorType=sensor_type,
â”‚                    Location=device.Location
â”‚                )
â”‚                session.add(sensor)
â”‚                sensors.append(sensor)
â”‚            session.flush()
â”‚            return sensors
â”‚        
â”‚        def insert_sensor_data(session: Session, sensors):
â”‚            now = datetime.utcnow()
â”‚            for sensor in sensors:
â”‚                for i in range(3):  # 3 entries per sensor
â”‚                    timestamp = now - timedelta(minutes=i)
â”‚                    value = round(random.uniform(20.0, 35.0), 2) if "Temp" in sensor.SensorType else round(random.uniform(30.0, 80.0), 2)
â”‚        
â”‚                    # Raw sensor data
â”‚                    sensor_data = SensorData(
â”‚                        SensorID=sensor.SensorID,
â”‚                        Timestamp=timestamp,
â”‚                        Value=value
â”‚                    )
â”‚                    session.add(sensor_data)
â”‚        
â”‚                    # Simulated Kalman output (slightly smoothed)
â”‚                    kalman_value = round(value + random.uniform(-1.0, 1.0), 2)
â”‚                    kalman_data = KalmanFilterFusionData(
â”‚                        SensorID=sensor.SensorID,
â”‚                        Timestamp=timestamp,
â”‚                        FusedValue=kalman_value
â”‚                    )
â”‚                    session.add(kalman_data)
â”‚        
â”‚        def create_dummy_actuators(session: Session, user, devices):
â”‚            for i, device in enumerate(devices):
â”‚                actuator = Actuator(
â”‚                    ActuatorName=f"Pump_{i+1}",
â”‚                    Status="Active" if i % 2 == 0 else "Inactive",
â”‚                    UserID=user.UserID,
â”‚                    DeviceID=device.DeviceID
â”‚                )
â”‚                session.add(actuator)
â”‚        
â”‚        def main():
â”‚            Base.metadata.create_all(engine)
â”‚            session = SessionLocal()
â”‚        
â”‚            try:
â”‚                print("[INFO] Populating database with dummy data...")
â”‚        
â”‚                user = create_dummy_user(session)
â”‚                devices = create_dummy_devices(session)
â”‚                sensors = create_dummy_sensors(session, devices)
â”‚                insert_sensor_data(session, sensors)
â”‚                create_dummy_actuators(session, user, devices)
â”‚        
â”‚                session.commit()
â”‚                print("[SUCCESS] Database populated successfully.")
â”‚        
â”‚            except Exception as e:
â”‚                session.rollback()
â”‚                print(f"[ERROR] Failed to populate database: {e}")
â”‚            finally:
â”‚                session.close()
â”‚        
â”‚        if __name__ == "__main__":
â”‚            main()

â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ database.py
â”‚        â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
â”‚        from sqlalchemy import create_engine, Column, Integer, Float, String, DateTime, ForeignKey
â”‚        from sqlalchemy.orm import relationship, sessionmaker, DeclarativeBase
â”‚        from datetime import datetime
â”‚        
â”‚        # âœ… SQLite Database Connection
â”‚        DATABASE_URL = "sqlite:///greenhouse.db"
â”‚        engine = create_engine(DATABASE_URL, echo=True)  # `echo=True` shows SQL logs
â”‚        
â”‚        # âœ… Base Model
â”‚        class Base(DeclarativeBase):
â”‚            pass
â”‚        
â”‚        # âœ… Devices Table (ESP32, ESP32-CAM, Raspberry Pi)
â”‚        class Device(Base):
â”‚            __tablename__ = "devices"
â”‚        
â”‚            id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
â”‚            name = Column(String, unique=True)
â”‚            type = Column(String)  # e.g., "ESP32", "ESP32-CAM", "Raspberry Pi"
â”‚            location = Column(String)  # e.g., "Greenhouse Zone 1"
â”‚        
â”‚            sensors = relationship("Sensor", back_populates="device")
â”‚        
â”‚        # âœ… Sensors Table (Temperature, Humidity, Soil Moisture)
â”‚        class Sensor(Base):
â”‚            __tablename__ = "sensors"
â”‚        
â”‚            id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
â”‚            device_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("devices.id"))
â”‚            type = Column(String)  # e.g., "temperature", "humidity", "soil_moisture"
â”‚            unit = Column(String)  # e.g., "Â°C", "%", "VWC"
â”‚        
â”‚            device = relationship("Device", back_populates="sensors")
â”‚            readings = relationship("SensorReading", back_populates="sensor")
â”‚        
â”‚        # âœ… Sensor Readings Table
â”‚        class SensorReading(Base):
â”‚            __tablename__ = "sensor_readings"
â”‚        
â”‚            id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
â”‚            sensor_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("sensors.id"))
â”‚            value = Column(Float)
â”‚            timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
â”‚        
â”‚            sensor = relationship("Sensor", back_populates="readings")
â”‚        
â”‚        # âœ… Users Table
â”‚        class User(Base):
â”‚            __tablename__ = "users"
â”‚        
â”‚            id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
â”‚            username = Column(String, unique=True)
â”‚            role = Column(String)  # e.g., "admin", "user"
â”‚            email = Column(String, unique=True)
â”‚        
â”‚            actions = relationship("UserAction", back_populates="user")
â”‚        
â”‚        # âœ… User Actions Table
â”‚        class UserAction(Base):
â”‚            __tablename__ = "user_actions"
â”‚        
â”‚            id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
â”‚            user_id = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("users.id"))
â”‚            action_type = Column(String)  # e.g., "turn_on_fan", "water_plants"
â”‚            action_value = Column(String)  # Any additional info (e.g., duration)
â”‚            timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
â”‚        
â”‚            user = relationship("User", back_populates="actions")
â”‚        
â”‚        # âœ… Weighted Averages Table (For Dashboards)
â”‚        class WeightedAverage(Base):
â”‚            __tablename__ = "weighted_averages"
â”‚        
â”‚            id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
â”‚            sensor_type = Column(String)  # "temperature", "humidity", "soil_moisture"
â”‚            weighted_value = Column(Float)
â”‚            timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
â”‚        
â”‚        # âœ… Create Tables in SQLite
â”‚        Base.metadata.create_all(engine)
â”‚        
â”‚        # âœ… Insert Test Data
â”‚        Session = sessionmaker(bind=engine)
â”‚        session = Session()
â”‚        
â”‚        # Adding sample devices
â”‚        device1 = Device(name="ESP32_1", type="ESP32", location="Greenhouse Zone 1")
â”‚        session.add(device1)
â”‚        
â”‚        # Adding sample sensors
â”‚        sensor1 = Sensor(device=device1, type="temperature", unit="Â°C")
â”‚        session.add(sensor1)
â”‚        
â”‚        # Adding sample sensor reading
â”‚        reading1 = SensorReading(sensor=sensor1, value=25.6)
â”‚        session.add(reading1)
â”‚        
â”‚        # Adding a test user
â”‚        user1 = User(username="admin", role="admin", email="admin@example.com")
â”‚        session.add(user1)
â”‚        
â”‚        # Adding a test user action
â”‚        action1 = UserAction(user=user1, action_type="water_plants", action_value="5 seconds")
â”‚        session.add(action1)
â”‚        
â”‚        # Committing the session
â”‚        session.commit()
â”‚        session.close()
â”‚        
â”‚        print("\nâœ… Database setup complete!")

â”‚        def show_table_structure(table_name):
â”‚            cursor.execute(f"PRAGMA table_info({table_name});")
â”‚            columns = cursor.fetchall()
â”‚            print(f"\n Structure of '{table_name}' table:")

â”‚                print(f"Column: {col[1]} | Type: {col[2]}")

â”‚            Timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
â”‚

â”œâ”€â”€ database_setup.py
     â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     from sqlalchemy import (
         create_engine, Column, Integer, Float, String, DateTime,
         ForeignKey, Boolean, Index
     )
     from sqlalchemy.orm import relationship, sessionmaker, declarative_base
     from datetime import datetime
     
     # Database connection
     DATABASE_URL = "sqlite:///greenhouse.db"
     engine = create_engine(DATABASE_URL, echo=True)
     SessionLocal = sessionmaker(bind=engine)
     
     # Base class
     Base = declarative_base()
     
     # UserCredentials Table
     class UserCredentials(Base):
         __tablename__ = "user_credentials"
     
         UserID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
         Username = Column(String(50), nullable=False, unique=True)
         PasswordHash = Column(String(128), nullable=False)
         Email = Column(String(100), nullable=False, unique=True)
         FullName = Column(String(100))
         CreatedAt = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
         IsActive = Column(Boolean, default=True)
     
         interactions = relationship("UserInteraction", back_populates="user", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
         actuators = relationship("Actuator", back_populates="user")
     
         def __repr__(self):
             return f"<UserCredentials(Username={self.Username}, Email={self.Email})>"
     
     # Devices Table
     class Device(Base):
         __tablename__ = "devices"
     
         DeviceID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, autoincrement=False)
         DeviceName = Column(String(50), nullable=False)
         Location = Column(String(100))
         Status = Column(String(20), default="Active")
     
         sensors = relationship("Sensor", back_populates="device", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
         user_interactions = relationship("UserInteraction", back_populates="device", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
         actuators = relationship("Actuator", back_populates="device", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
     
         def __repr__(self):
             return f"<Device(Name={self.DeviceName}, Location={self.Location})>"
     
     # Sensors Table â€” NO UNIQUE CONSTRAINTS
     class Sensor(Base):
         __tablename__ = "sensors"
     
         SensorID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True, autoincrement=False)
         DeviceID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("devices.DeviceID"), nullable=False)
         SensorType = Column(String(50), nullable=False)
         Location = Column(String(100))
         Status = Column(String(20), default="Active")
     
         device = relationship("Device", back_populates="sensors")
         sensor_data = relationship("SensorData", back_populates="sensor", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
         kalmanFilterFusionData = relationship("KalmanFilterFusionData", back_populates="sensor", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
     
         def __repr__(self):
             return f"<Sensor(SensorID={self.SensorID}, Type={self.SensorType}, Location={self.Location})>"
     
     # Sensor Data Table
     class SensorData(Base):
         __tablename__ = "sensor_data"
         __table_args__ = (
             Index("ix_sensor_data_sensorid_timestamp", "SensorID", "Timestamp"),
         )
     
         DataID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
         SensorID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("sensors.SensorID"), nullable=False)
         Timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
         Value = Column(Float, nullable=False)
     
         sensor = relationship("Sensor", back_populates="sensor_data")
     
         def __repr__(self):
             return f"<SensorData(SensorID={self.SensorID}, Value={self.Value})>"
     
     # Kalman Filter Fusion Table
     class KalmanFilterFusionData(Base):
         __tablename__ = "kalman_filter_fusion"
     
         FusionID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
         SensorID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("sensors.SensorID"), nullable=False)
         Timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
         FusedValue = Column(Float, nullable=False)
     
         sensor = relationship("Sensor", back_populates="kalmanFilterFusionData")
     
         def __repr__(self):
             return f"<KalmanFusion(SensorID={self.SensorID}, Value={self.FusedValue})>"
     
     # Weighted Average Fusion Table
     class WeightedAverageFusionData(Base):
         __tablename__ = "weighted_average_fusion"
     
         FusionID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
         SensorType = Column(String(50), nullable=False)
         Timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
         FusedValue = Column(Float, nullable=False)
     
         def __repr__(self):
             return f"<WeightedFusion(SensorType={self.SensorType}, Value={self.FusedValue})>"
     
     # Actuators Table
     class Actuator(Base):
         __tablename__ = "actuators"
     
         ActuatorID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
         ActuatorName = Column(String(50), nullable=False, unique=True)
         Status = Column(String(20), nullable=False, default="Inactive")
         LastUpdated = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
         UserID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("user_credentials.UserID"))
         DeviceID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("devices.DeviceID"))
     
         interactions = relationship("UserInteraction", back_populates="actuator")
         user = relationship("UserCredentials", back_populates="actuators")
         device = relationship("Device", back_populates="actuators")
     
         def __repr__(self):
             return f"<Actuator(Name={self.ActuatorName}, Status={self.Status})>"
     
     # User Interactions Table
     class UserInteraction(Base):
         __tablename__ = "user_interactions"
     
         InteractionID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
         UserID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("user_credentials.UserID"), nullable=False)
         DeviceID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("devices.DeviceID"), nullable=False)
         ActuatorID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("actuators.ActuatorID"))
         Action = Column(String(20), nullable=False)
         Timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
     
         user = relationship("UserCredentials", back_populates="interactions")
         device = relationship("Device", back_populates="user_interactions")
         actuator = relationship("Actuator", back_populates="interactions")
     
         def __repr__(self):
             return f"<UserInteraction(UserID={self.UserID}, DeviceID={self.DeviceID}, Action={self.Action})>"
     
     # Create all tables
     Base.metadata.create_all(engine)
     â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

â”œâ”€â”€ directoryvis.py
     â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     import os
     
     # Set your root directory
     ROOT_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
     OUTPUT_FILE = os.path.join(ROOT_DIR, 'project_tree_output.txt')
     
     # File types to include for content printing
     ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS = {
         '.py', '.html', '.json', '.css', '.js', '.txt', '.md', '.csv'
     }
     
     def print_tree(path, prefix='', output_lines=None):
         """Recursively builds a tree view of the directory with file contents."""
         if output_lines is None:
             output_lines = []
     
         try:
             contents = sorted(os.listdir(path))
         except Exception as e:
             output_lines.append(prefix + f"[Error accessing {path}]: {e}")
             return output_lines
     
         pointers = ['â”œâ”€â”€ '] * (len(contents) - 1) + ['â””â”€â”€ ']
         for pointer, name in zip(pointers, contents):
             full_path = os.path.join(path, name)
             output_lines.append(prefix + pointer + name)
     
             if os.path.isdir(full_path):
                 extension = 'â”‚   ' if pointer == 'â”œâ”€â”€ ' else '    '
                 print_tree(full_path, prefix + extension, output_lines)
             else:
                 _, ext = os.path.splitext(name)
                 if ext.lower() in ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS:
                     try:
                         with open(full_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                             output_lines.append(prefix + '     â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“')
                             for line in f:
                                 output_lines.append(prefix + '     ' + line.rstrip())
                             output_lines.append(prefix + '     â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘\n')
                     except Exception as e:
                         output_lines.append(prefix + f'     [Error reading file: {e}]\n')
         return output_lines
     
     if __name__ == '__main__':
         tree_output = ['.']
         tree_output = print_tree(ROOT_DIR, output_lines=tree_output)
     
         # Write to file
         with open(OUTPUT_FILE, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
             f.write('\n'.join(tree_output))
     
         # Print file content
         with open(OUTPUT_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
             print(f.read())
     â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

â”‚        import cv2
â”‚        import requests
â”‚        import numpy as np
â”‚        import time
â”‚        
â”‚        # MJPEG stream URL
â”‚        url = "http://192.168.200.76:5000/video_feed"
â”‚        
â”‚        # Connect to the stream
â”‚        stream = requests.get(url, stream=True)
â”‚        if stream.status_code != 200:
â”‚            print("âŒ Failed to connect to video stream")
â”‚            exit()
â”‚        
â”‚        print("ğŸ“· Press 'b' to capture an image, 'q' to quit")
â”‚        
â”‚        bytes_buffer = b""
â”‚        img_count = 0
â”‚        
â”‚        for chunk in stream.iter_content(chunk_size=1024):
â”‚            bytes_buffer += chunk
â”‚            a = bytes_buffer.find(b'\xff\xd8')
â”‚            b = bytes_buffer.find(b'\xff\xd9')
â”‚        
â”‚            if a != -1 and b != -1:
â”‚                jpg = bytes_buffer[a:b+2]
â”‚                bytes_buffer = bytes_buffer[b+2:]
â”‚        
â”‚                img_np = np.frombuffer(jpg, dtype=np.uint8)
â”‚                frame = cv2.imdecode(img_np, cv2.IMREAD_COLOR)
â”‚                frame = cv2.cvtColor(frame, cv2.COLOR_BGR2RGB)
â”‚        
â”‚                if frame is not None:
â”‚                    cv2.imshow("Live Stream", frame)
â”‚        
â”‚                    key = cv2.waitKey(1) & 0xFF
â”‚                    if key == ord('b'):
â”‚                        filename = f"snapshot_{int(time.time())}.jpg"
â”‚                        cv2.imwrite(filename, frame)
â”‚                        print(f"âœ… Saved snapshot as {filename}")
â”‚                    elif key == ord('q'):
â”‚                        print("ğŸ‘‹ Exiting...")
â”‚                        break
â”‚        
â”‚        cv2.destroyAllWindows()

â”œâ”€â”€ kalman_filter_readings_4_weighted_AVG.py
     â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     from datetime import timedelta
     import pandas as pd
     from database_setup import SessionLocal, KalmanFilterFusionData
     
     # Start DB session
     session: Session = SessionLocal()
     
     # Step 1: Get latest timestamp
     latest_entry = session.query(KalmanFilterFusionData).order_by(
         KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp.desc()
     ).first()
     
     if latest_entry:
         latest_timestamp = latest_entry.Timestamp
         start_timestamp = latest_timestamp - timedelta(minutes=20)
     
         # Step 2: Query data within the latest 20-minute window
         results = session.query(KalmanFilterFusionData).filter(
             KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp.between(start_timestamp, latest_timestamp)
         ).order_by(KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp.asc()).all()
     
         # Step 3: Convert to DataFrame
         df = pd.DataFrame([{
             "Timestamp": r.Timestamp,
             f"{r.SensorID}": r.FusedValue
         } for r in results])
     
         # Step 4: Pivot based on SensorID (aggregated on Timestamp)
         df_pivoted = df.pivot_table(
             index="Timestamp",
             aggfunc="first"  # If multiple values exist per sensor & timestamp, take the first
         )
     
         # Optional: sort columns by SensorID
         df_pivoted = df_pivoted[sorted(df_pivoted.columns, key=int)]
     
         # Step 5: Save to CSV
         df_pivoted.to_csv("kalman_latest_20min_pivoted.csv")
         print("âœ… Pivoted CSV 'kalman_latest_20min_pivoted.csv' saved.")
     else:
         print("âš ï¸ No data found in KalmanFilterFusionData.")
     
     # Step 6: Close DB session
     session.close()
     â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

â”œâ”€â”€ network.py
     â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     from flask import request, jsonify
     from time import sleep
     from datetime import datetime
     import logging
     
     from network_utils.auth import authenticate_request
     from network_utils.sensor_storage import store_sensor_data
     from network_utils.fusion_utils import get_latest_fused_temperature_humidity, get_fused_values_by_sensors
     from network_utils.actions import action_based_on_sensor
     from network_utils.constants import soil_sensor_1id, soil_sensor_2id
     from database_setup import SessionLocal, Actuator
     
     # Configure logging
     logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
     logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
     
     def receive_sensor_data(request):
         if not authenticate_request(request):
             return jsonify({"error": "Unauthorized"}), 401
     
         try:
             data = request.get_json()
             print(f"Recived paylaod: {data}")
             if not data:
                 return jsonify({"error": "Invalid or missing JSON payload"}), 400
     
             time = datetime.utcnow()
             device_id = data.get('DeviceID')
             device_name = data.get('DeviceName')
             actuator_id = data.get('ActuatorID')
             actuator_status = data.get('ActuatorState')
             sensor_ids = data.get("SensorID", [])
     
             temperatures = data.get("temperature", [])
             filtered_temperatures = data.get("filtered_temperature", [])
             humidities = data.get("humidity", [])
             filtered_humidities = data.get("filtered_humidity", [])
             soil_moistures = data.get("soil_moisture", [])
             filtered_soil_moistures = data.get("filtered_soil_moisture", [])
     
             with SessionLocal() as session:
                 for i, sensor_id in enumerate(sensor_ids):
                     if i < len(temperatures) and i < len(filtered_temperatures):
                         if temperatures[i] > 0 and filtered_temperatures[i] > 0:
                             store_sensor_data(session, device_id, device_name, sensor_id,
                                               temperature=temperatures[i],
                                               filtered_temperature=filtered_temperatures[i],
                                               timestamp=time)
     
                     if i < len(humidities) and i < len(filtered_humidities):
                         if humidities[i] > 0 and filtered_humidities[i] > 0:
                             store_sensor_data(session, device_id, device_name, sensor_id,
                                               humidity=humidities[i],
                                               filtered_humidity=filtered_humidities[i],
                                               timestamp=time)
     
                     if i < len(soil_moistures) and i < len(filtered_soil_moistures):
                         if soil_moistures[i] > 0 and filtered_soil_moistures[i] > 0:
                             store_sensor_data(session, device_id, device_name, sensor_id,
                                               soil_moisture=soil_moistures[i],
                                               filtered_soil_moisture=filtered_soil_moistures[i],
                                               timestamp=time)
     
                     logger.info(f"Received data from DeviceID: {device_id}, SensorID: {sensor_id}")
     
                 # Handle actuator state
                 if actuator_id is not None and actuator_status is not None:
                     actuator = session.query(Actuator).filter(Actuator.ActuatorID == actuator_id).first()
                     if actuator:
                         actuator.Status = actuator_status
                         actuator.LastUpdated = time
                         logger.info(f"Updated Actuator {actuator_id} to {actuator_status}")
                         session.commit()
                     else:
                         try:
                             new_actuator = Actuator(
                                 ActuatorID=actuator_id,
                                 ActuatorName=f"Auto_Actuator_{actuator_id}",
                                 Status=actuator_status,
                                 UserID=5000,  # Automatic control
                                 DeviceID=device_id,
                                 LastUpdated=time
                             )
                             session.add(new_actuator)
                             logger.info(f"Created new Actuator with ID {actuator_id} and status {actuator_status}")
                         except Exception as e:
                             session.rollback()
                             logger.warning(f"Failed to insert new actuator â€” error: {e}")
     
                 action_result = action_based_on_sensor()
     
                 latest = get_latest_fused_temperature_humidity(session)
                 soil_data = get_fused_values_by_sensors(session, soil_sensor_1id, soil_sensor_2id)
                 avg_soil = sum(soil_data.values()) / len(soil_data) if soil_data else None
     
                 session.commit()
     
             sleep(5)  # Optional delay
     
             return jsonify({
                 "status": "success",
                 "action": action_result,
                 "temperature": latest.get("temperature"),
                 "humidity": latest.get("humidity"),
                 "soil_moisture": avg_soil
             }), 200
     
         except Exception as e:
             logger.error(f"Failed to receive/process sensor data: {e}")
             return jsonify({"error": "Internal Server Error"}), 500
     
     
     â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

â”‚        â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
â”‚        from .fusion_utils import get_fused_values_by_sensors
â”‚        from .actuator_control import control_actuator
â”‚        from .config_handler import load_config
â”‚        from weightedAverage import process_weighted_fusion
â”‚        from database_setup import SessionLocal, WeightedAverageFusionData
â”‚        from .constants import *
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚        def action_based_on_sensor(user_id=DEFAULT_USER_ID):
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] action.py loaded successfully.")
â”‚        
â”‚            # Load dynamic thresholds
â”‚            config = load_config()
â”‚            TEMP_THRESHOLD = config.get("TEMP_THRESHOLD", 27)
â”‚            HUM_THRESHOLD = config.get("HUM_THRESHOLD", 80)
â”‚            SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD = config.get("SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD", 4000)
â”‚        
â”‚            with SessionLocal() as session:
â”‚                # Get fused soil moisture readings
â”‚                result = get_fused_values_by_sensors(session, soil_sensor_1id, soil_sensor_2id)
â”‚                soil1 = result.get(soil_sensor_1id)
â”‚                soil2 = result.get(soil_sensor_2id)
â”‚                soil_moisture = None
â”‚        
â”‚                if soil1 is not None and soil2 is not None:
â”‚                    avg = (soil1 + soil2) / 2
â”‚                    if 0 <= avg <= 5000:
â”‚                        soil_moisture = avg
â”‚                elif soil1 and 0 <= soil1 <= 5000:
â”‚                    soil_moisture = soil1
â”‚                elif soil2 and 0 <= soil2 <= 5000:
â”‚                    soil_moisture = soil2
â”‚                else:
â”‚                    print("[WARNING] Invalid soil moisture readings, using None.")
â”‚        
â”‚                # Update fusion values
â”‚                process_weighted_fusion(sensor_ids=TEMP_SENSOR_IDS, weights=WEIGHTS, sensor_type="temperature")
â”‚                process_weighted_fusion(sensor_ids=HUM_SENSOR_IDS, weights=WEIGHTS, sensor_type="humidity")
â”‚        
â”‚                # Get latest temperature
â”‚                temperature_record = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData) \
â”‚                    .filter(WeightedAverageFusionData.SensorType == "temperature") \
â”‚                    .order_by(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp.desc()) \
â”‚                    .first()
â”‚                temperature = temperature_record.FusedValue if temperature_record else None
â”‚                if temperature is None:
â”‚                    print("[WARNING] No temperature data found.")
â”‚        
â”‚                # Get latest humidity
â”‚                humidity_record = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData) \
â”‚                    .filter(WeightedAverageFusionData.SensorType == "humidity") \
â”‚                    .order_by(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp.desc()) \
â”‚                    .first()
â”‚                humidity = humidity_record.FusedValue if humidity_record else None
â”‚                if humidity is None:
â”‚                    print("[WARNING] No humidity data found.")
â”‚        
â”‚                actions = []
â”‚        
â”‚                try:
â”‚                    # --- VENTILATION CONTROL ---
â”‚                    if temperature is not None and humidity is not None:
â”‚                        if temperature > TEMP_THRESHOLD or humidity > HUM_THRESHOLD:
â”‚                            control_actuator(session, VENTILATION_FAN, "on", user_id)
â”‚                            control_actuator(session, INTAKE_SHUTTER, "on", user_id)
â”‚                            actions.append("Ventilation_ON")
â”‚                        else:
â”‚                            control_actuator(session, VENTILATION_FAN, "off", user_id)
â”‚                            control_actuator(session, INTAKE_SHUTTER, "off", user_id)
â”‚                            actions.append("Ventilation_OFF")
â”‚        
â”‚                    # --- IRRIGATION CONTROL ---
â”‚                    if soil_moisture is not None:
â”‚                        if soil_moisture < SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD:
â”‚                            control_actuator(session, WATER_PUMP, "on", user_id)
â”‚                            actions.append("Irrigation_ON")
â”‚                        else:
â”‚                            control_actuator(session, WATER_PUMP, "off", user_id)
â”‚                            actions.append("Irrigation_OFF")
â”‚        
â”‚                    session.commit()
â”‚                    print("[DEBUG] actions.py [WORKED]")
â”‚                    print(f"[DEBUG] Thresholds: TEMP={TEMP_THRESHOLD}, HUM={HUM_THRESHOLD}, SOIL={SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD}")
â”‚                    print(f"[DEBUG] Readings: TEMP={temperature}, HUM={humidity}, SOIL={soil_moisture}")
â”‚                    print(f"[DEBUG] Actions performed: {actions}")
â”‚                    return ", ".join(actions) if actions else "none"
â”‚        
â”‚                except Exception as e:
â”‚                    session.rollback()
â”‚                    print(f"[ERROR] Failed to perform action: {e}")
â”‚                    return "error"
â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ actuator_control.py

â”‚        from datetime import datetime
â”‚        from database_setup import Actuator, UserInteraction
â”‚        
â”‚        def log_user_action(session, device_id, action, user_id, actuator_id):
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] actuator_control.py/log_user_action loaded successfully.")
â”‚            session.add(UserInteraction(
â”‚                DeviceID=device_id,
â”‚                Action=action,
â”‚                UserID=user_id,
â”‚                ActuatorID=actuator_id,
â”‚                Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] actuator_control.py/log_user_action loaded successfully [WORKED].")
â”‚        
â”‚        def control_actuator(session, actuator_name, status, user_id):
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] actuator_control.py/control_actuator loaded successfully.")
â”‚            actuator = session.query(Actuator).filter_by(ActuatorName=actuator_name).first()
â”‚            if not actuator:
â”‚                actuator = Actuator(ActuatorName=actuator_name, Status=status, LastUpdated=datetime.utcnow(), UserID=user_id)
â”‚                session.add(actuator)
â”‚            else:
â”‚                if actuator.Status != status:
â”‚                    actuator.Status = status
â”‚                    actuator.LastUpdated = datetime.utcnow()
â”‚                    actuator.UserID = user_id
â”‚                    log_user_action(session, actuator.ActuatorID, f"{actuator_name}_{status.lower()}", user_id, actuator.ActuatorID)
â”‚            session.commit()
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] actuator_control.py/control_actuator loaded successfully [WORKED].")
â”‚            return actuator

â”‚        from flask import request, jsonify, Blueprint, render_template, redirect, url_for, flash, session
â”‚        from werkzeug.security import generate_password_hash, check_password_hash
â”‚        from database_setup import SessionLocal, UserCredentials
â”‚        from .constants import credentials
â”‚        
â”‚        def authenticate_request(request):
â”‚            auth = request.authorization
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] auth.py loaded successfully.")
â”‚            if not auth or credentials.get(auth.username) != auth.password:
â”‚                return False
â”‚            return True
â”‚        
â”‚        auth_bp = Blueprint('auth', __name__)
â”‚        
â”‚        @auth_bp.route("/signup", methods=["GET", "POST"])
â”‚        def signup():
â”‚            if request.method == "POST":
â”‚                email = request.form.get("email")
â”‚                username = request.form.get("username")
â”‚                full_name = request.form.get("full_name")
â”‚                password = request.form.get("password")
â”‚        
â”‚                db = SessionLocal()
â”‚                existing_user = db.query(UserCredentials).filter_by(Email=email).first()
â”‚        
â”‚                if existing_user:
â”‚                    flash("Email already exists.", "error")
â”‚                    db.close()
â”‚                    return redirect(url_for("auth.signup"))
â”‚        
â”‚                hashed_pw = generate_password_hash(password)
â”‚                new_user = UserCredentials(
â”‚                    Email=email,
â”‚                    Username=username,
â”‚                    FullName=full_name,
â”‚                    PasswordHash=hashed_pw
â”‚                )
â”‚                db.add(new_user)
â”‚                db.commit()
â”‚                db.close()
â”‚        
â”‚                flash("Account created! Please log in.", "success")
â”‚                return redirect(url_for("auth.login"))
â”‚        
â”‚            return render_template("signup.html",hide_nav=True)
â”‚        
â”‚        @auth_bp.route("/login", methods=["GET", "POST"])
â”‚        def login():
â”‚            if request.method == "POST":
â”‚                email = request.form.get("email")
â”‚                password = request.form.get("password")
â”‚        
â”‚                db = SessionLocal()
â”‚                user = db.query(UserCredentials).filter_by(Email=email).first()
â”‚        
â”‚                if user and check_password_hash(user.PasswordHash, password):
â”‚                    session["user_id"] = user.UserID
â”‚                    session["username"] = user.Username
â”‚                    session.permanent = False  # ğŸŸ¢ Session ends when browser/tab closes
â”‚                    db.close()
â”‚                    flash("Login successful!", "success")
â”‚                    return redirect(url_for("index"))
â”‚                else:
â”‚                    flash("Invalid email or password.", "error")
â”‚                    db.close()
â”‚                    return redirect(url_for("auth.login"))
â”‚        
â”‚            return render_template("login.html", hide_nav=True)
â”‚        
â”‚        @auth_bp.route("/logout", methods=["GET", "POST"])
â”‚        def logout():
â”‚            session.clear()
â”‚        
â”‚            if request.method == "POST":
â”‚                return "", 204  # for navigator.sendBeacon()
â”‚        
â”‚            flash("Logged out successfully.", "info")
â”‚            return redirect(url_for("auth.login"))

â”‚        import json
â”‚        import os
â”‚        
â”‚        CONFIG_PATH = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), 'config.json')
â”‚        
â”‚        def load_config():
â”‚            if not os.path.exists(CONFIG_PATH):
â”‚                # Return default config if the file doesn't exist
â”‚                return {
â”‚                    "TEMP_THRESHOLD": 27,
â”‚                    "HUM_THRESHOLD": 80,
â”‚                    "SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD": 4000
â”‚                }
â”‚            with open(CONFIG_PATH, 'r') as file:
â”‚                return json.load(file)
â”‚        
â”‚        def save_config(config):
â”‚            with open(CONFIG_PATH, 'w') as file:
â”‚                json.dump(config, file, indent=4)
â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

â”‚        from database_setup import Device, Sensor
â”‚        from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
â”‚        
â”‚        def get_or_create_device(session: Session, device_id, device_name):
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] device_utils.py/get_or_create_device loaded successfully.")
â”‚            device = session.query(Device).filter_by(DeviceID=device_id).first()
â”‚            if not device:
â”‚                device = Device(DeviceID=device_id, DeviceName=device_name, Location="Unknown", Status="Active")
â”‚                session.add(device)
â”‚                session.commit()
â”‚                session.refresh(device)
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] device_utils.py/get_or_create_device[WORKED].")
â”‚            return device
â”‚        
â”‚        def get_or_create_sensor(session: Session, sensor_id, device_id, sensor_type):
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] device_utils.py/get_or_create_sensor loaded successfully.")
â”‚        
â”‚            sensor = session.query(Sensor).filter_by(SensorID=sensor_id).first()
â”‚            if not sensor:
â”‚                # Create new sensor if none exists with this SensorID
â”‚                sensor = Sensor(SensorID=sensor_id, DeviceID=device_id, SensorType=sensor_type, Location="Unknown", Status="Active")
â”‚                session.add(sensor)
â”‚                session.commit()
â”‚                session.refresh(sensor)
â”‚            else:
â”‚                # Optionally update sensor_type or other fields if different
â”‚                if sensor.SensorType != sensor_type:
â”‚                    sensor.SensorType = sensor_type
â”‚                    session.commit()
â”‚        
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] device_utils.py/get_or_create_sensor[WORKED].")
â”‚            return sensor
â”‚

â”‚        from sqlalchemy import desc
â”‚        from database_setup import KalmanFilterFusionData, WeightedAverageFusionData
â”‚        
â”‚        def get_fused_values_by_sensors(session, *sensor_ids):
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] fusion_utils.py/get_fused_values_by_sensors loaded successfully.")
â”‚            print(f"[DEBUG] fusion_utils.py/get_fused_values_by_sensors called with sensor_ids: {sensor_ids}")
â”‚            fused = {}
â”‚            for sensor_id in sensor_ids:
â”‚                fusion = session.query(KalmanFilterFusionData).filter_by(SensorID=sensor_id).order_by(desc(KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp)).first()
â”‚                if fusion:
â”‚                    fused[sensor_id] = fusion.FusedValue
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] fusion_utils.py/get_fused_values_by_sensors [WORKED].")
â”‚            return fused
â”‚        
â”‚        def get_latest_fused_temperature_humidity(session):
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] fusion_utils.py/get_latest_fused_temperature_humidity loaded successfully.")
â”‚            temp = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData).filter_by(SensorType="temperature").order_by(desc(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp)).first()
â”‚            hum = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData).filter_by(SensorType="humidity").order_by(desc(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp)).first()
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] fusion_utils.py/get_latest_fused_temperature_humidity [WORKED].")
â”‚            return {
â”‚                "temperature": temp.FusedValue if temp else None,
â”‚                "humidity": hum.FusedValue if hum else None
â”‚            }

â”‚        from datetime import datetime
â”‚        from database_setup import SensorData, KalmanFilterFusionData
â”‚        from .device_utils import get_or_create_device, get_or_create_sensor
â”‚        
â”‚        def store_sensor_value(session, sensor, value, time):
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] sensor_storage.py/store_sensor_value loaded successfully.")
â”‚            session.add(SensorData(SensorID=sensor.SensorID, Value=value, Timestamp=time))
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] sensor_storage.py/store_sensor_value [WORKED].")
â”‚        
â”‚        def store_sensor_fused_value(session, sensor, value, time):
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] sensor_storage.py/store_sensor_fused_value loaded successfully.")
â”‚            session.add(KalmanFilterFusionData(SensorID=sensor.SensorID, FusedValue=value, Timestamp=time))
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] sensor_storage.py/store_sensor_fused_value [WORKED].")
â”‚        
â”‚        def store_sensor_data(session, device_id, device_name, sensor_id,
â”‚                              temperature=None, filtered_temperature=None,
â”‚                              humidity=None, filtered_humidity=None,
â”‚                              soil_moisture=None, filtered_soil_moisture=None, timestamp=None):
â”‚            get_or_create_device(session, device_id, device_name)
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] sensor_storage.py/store_sensor_data loaded successfully.")
â”‚            if temperature is not None:
â”‚                sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, sensor_id, device_id, "temperature")
â”‚                store_sensor_value(session, sensor, temperature, timestamp)
â”‚            if filtered_temperature is not None:
â”‚                sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, sensor_id, device_id, "temperature")
â”‚                store_sensor_fused_value(session, sensor, filtered_temperature, timestamp)
â”‚            if humidity is not None:
â”‚                sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, sensor_id, device_id, "humidity")
â”‚                store_sensor_value(session, sensor, humidity, timestamp)
â”‚            if filtered_humidity is not None:
â”‚                sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, sensor_id, device_id, "humidity_filtered")
â”‚                store_sensor_fused_value(session, sensor, filtered_humidity, timestamp)
â”‚            if soil_moisture is not None:
â”‚                sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, sensor_id, device_id, "soil_moisture")
â”‚                store_sensor_value(session, sensor, soil_moisture,timestamp)
â”‚            if filtered_soil_moisture is not None:
â”‚                sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, sensor_id, device_id, "soil_moisture_filtered")
â”‚                store_sensor_fused_value(session, sensor, filtered_soil_moisture, timestamp)
â”‚            session.commit()
â”‚            print("[DEBUG] sensor_storage.py/store_sensor_data [WORKED].")
â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

â”‚        â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
â”‚        from flask import Blueprint, render_template, jsonify
â”‚        from .fusion_utils import get_fused_values_by_sensors
â”‚        from database_setup import SessionLocal, WeightedAverageFusionData
â”‚        from .constants import soil_sensor_1id, soil_sensor_2id
â”‚        
â”‚        status_bp = Blueprint('status', __name__)
â”‚        
â”‚        @status_bp.route("/status")
â”‚        def status_page():
â”‚            return render_template("index.html")
â”‚        
â”‚        @status_bp.route("/api/latest-fused-values")
â”‚        def latest_fused_values():
â”‚            temperature = None
â”‚            humidity = None
â”‚            soil_moisture = None
â”‚        
â”‚            try:
â”‚                with SessionLocal() as session:
â”‚                    # --- Latest Soil Moisture ---
â”‚                    result = get_fused_values_by_sensors(session, soil_sensor_1id, soil_sensor_2id)
â”‚                    soil1 = result.get(soil_sensor_1id)
â”‚                    soil2 = result.get(soil_sensor_2id)
â”‚        
â”‚                    valid_soil_values = [v for v in [soil1, soil2] if v is not None and 0 <= v <= 5000]
â”‚                    if valid_soil_values:
â”‚                        soil_moisture = sum(valid_soil_values) / len(valid_soil_values)
â”‚                    else:
â”‚                        print("[WARNING] No valid soil moisture readings found.")
â”‚        
â”‚                    # --- Latest Temperature ---
â”‚                    temp_record = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData)\
â”‚                        .filter(WeightedAverageFusionData.SensorType == "temperature")\
â”‚                        .order_by(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp.desc())\
â”‚                        .first()
â”‚        
â”‚                    if temp_record:
â”‚                        temperature = temp_record.FusedValue
â”‚                    else:
â”‚                        print("[WARNING] No temperature data found.")
â”‚        
â”‚                    # --- Latest Humidity ---
â”‚                    hum_record = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData)\
â”‚                        .filter(WeightedAverageFusionData.SensorType == "humidity")\
â”‚                        .order_by(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp.desc())\
â”‚                        .first()
â”‚        
â”‚                    if hum_record:
â”‚                        humidity = hum_record.FusedValue
â”‚                    else:
â”‚                        print("[WARNING] No humidity data found.")
â”‚        
â”‚            except Exception as e:
â”‚                print(f"[ERROR] Failed to fetch latest fused values: {e}")
â”‚        
â”‚            return jsonify({
â”‚                "temperature": temperature,
â”‚                "humidity": humidity,
â”‚                "soil_moisture": soil_moisture
â”‚            })
â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

â”‚   â””â”€â”€ user_control.py
â”‚        â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
â”‚        from datetime import datetime
â”‚        from database_setup import UserInteraction, SessionLocal, Actuator
â”‚        
â”‚        def handle_manual_control(payload):
â”‚        
â”‚            user_id = payload.get("user_id")
â”‚            actuator_id = payload.get("actuator_id")
â”‚            action = payload.get("action")
â”‚            time = datetime.utcnow()
â”‚        
â”‚            if not all([user_id, actuator_id, action]):
â”‚                return {"status": "error", "message": "Missing required fields"}
â”‚        
â”‚            with SessionLocal() as session:
â”‚                actuator = session.query(Actuator).filter(Actuator.ActuatorID == actuator_id).first()
â”‚                if not actuator:
â”‚                    actuator = Actuator(
â”‚                        ActuatorID=actuator_id,
â”‚                        ActuatorName=f"Manual_Actuator_{actuator_id}",
â”‚                        Status=action,
â”‚                        UserID=user_id,
â”‚                        LastUpdated=time
â”‚                    )
â”‚                    session.add(actuator)
â”‚                else:
â”‚                    actuator.Status = action
â”‚                    actuator.UserID = user_id
â”‚                    actuator.LastUpdated = time
â”‚        
â”‚                try:
â”‚                    device_id = actuator.DeviceID if actuator.DeviceID else 1001  # fallback
â”‚                    session.add(UserInteraction(
â”‚                        UserID=user_id,
â”‚                        DeviceID=device_id,
â”‚                        ActuatorID=actuator_id,
â”‚                        Action=action,
â”‚                        Timestamp=time
â”‚                    ))
â”‚                    session.commit()
â”‚                    return {"status": "success", "message": f"Manual action '{action}' recorded."}
â”‚                except Exception as e:
â”‚                    session.rollback()
â”‚                    return {"status": "error", "message": str(e)}

          import os
          import cv2
          from ultralytics import YOLO
     
          # Load YOLO model once
          model = YOLO('best.pt')
          print("[INFO] Model loaded. Classes:", model.names)
     
          def process_frame(frame):
              results = model(frame)
              for result in results:
                  for box in result.boxes:
                      x1, y1, x2, y2 = map(int, box.xyxy[0])
                      conf = box.conf[0].item()
                      cls = int(box.cls[0].item())
                      class_name = model.names.get(cls, f'Class {cls}')
                      label = f'{class_name} {conf:.2f}'
     
                      cv2.rectangle(frame, (x1, y1), (x2, y2), (0, 255, 0), 2)
                      (w, h), _ = cv2.getTextSize(label, cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX, 0.7, 2)
                      cv2.rectangle(frame, (x1, y1 - h - 5), (x1 + w, y1), (0, 255, 0), -1)
                      cv2.putText(frame, label, (x1, y1), cv2.FONT_HERSHEY_SIMPLEX,
                                  0.7, (0, 0, 0), 2, cv2.LINE_AA)
              return frame
     
          def process_images_in_directory(input_dir, output_dir):
              os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)
              supported_ext = ['.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.bmp']
     
              for filename in os.listdir(input_dir):
                  if any(filename.lower().endswith(ext) for ext in supported_ext):
                      image_path = os.path.join(input_dir, filename)
                      frame = cv2.imread(image_path)
                      if frame is None:
                          print(f"[WARNING] Couldn't read {filename}, skipping.")
                          continue
     
                      processed_frame = process_frame(frame)
                      output_path = os.path.join(output_dir, filename)
                      cv2.imwrite(output_path, processed_frame)
                      print(f"[INFO] Processed and saved: {output_path}")
     
          if __name__ == '__main__':
              process_images_in_directory('input', 'static/predictions')
          â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

          from flask import Flask, render_template, request, jsonify, url_for, redirect
          from dashboard import dashboard_bp
          from network_utils.status import status_bp
          from network import receive_sensor_data
          from AI_model import process_images_in_directory
          import os
          from network_utils.config_handler import load_config, save_config
     
          app = Flask(__name__)
     
          # Folders for image input/output
          INPUT_DIR = 'input'
          OUTPUT_DIR = 'static/predictions'
     
          # Register blueprints
          app.register_blueprint(dashboard_bp)
          app.register_blueprint(status_bp)
     
          @app.route('/')
          def index():
              return render_template('index.html')
     
          @app.route('/run', methods=['POST'])
          def run_yolo():
              process_images_in_directory(INPUT_DIR, OUTPUT_DIR)
              return redirect(url_for('ai_model'))
     
          @app.route('/results')
          def ai_model():
              images = [
                  f for f in os.listdir(OUTPUT_DIR)
                  if f.lower().endswith(('.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.bmp'))
              ]
              return render_template('ai_model.html', images=images)
     
          @app.route('/receive', methods=['POST'])
          def receive_data():
              return receive_sensor_data(request)
     
          @app.route('/get_thresholds')
          def get_thresholds():
              return jsonify(load_config())
     
          @app.route('/set_thresholds', methods=['POST'])
          def set_thresholds():
              data = request.get_json()
              try:
                  config = load_config()
                  config["TEMP_THRESHOLD"] = int(data.get("temp_threshold", config["TEMP_THRESHOLD"]))
                  config["HUM_THRESHOLD"] = int(data.get("hum_threshold", config["HUM_THRESHOLD"]))
                  config["SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD"] = int(data.get("soil_moisture_threshold", config["SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD"]))
                  save_config(config)
                  print("[DEBUG] Thresholds updated:", config)
                  return jsonify({"message": "Thresholds updated successfully."})
              except Exception as e:
                  return jsonify({"message": f"Error: {str(e)}"}), 400
     
          if __name__ == '__main__':
              app.run(host='0.0.0.0', port=5000)

          from flask import Blueprint, render_template, jsonify
          from database_setup import SessionLocal, SensorData, KalmanFilterFusionData, WeightedAverageFusionData
          from collections import defaultdict
          import json
     
          dashboard_bp = Blueprint('dashboard', __name__)
     
          sensor_labels = {
              2001: "Temperature - DHT1 Internal",
              2002: "Humidity - DHT1 Internal",
              2003: "Temperature - DHT2 Internal",
              2004: "Humidity - DHT2 Internal",
              2005: "Soil Moisture - Plant 1",
              3001: "Temperature - DHT3 Internal",
              3002: "Humidity - DHT3 Internal",
              3003: "Temperature - DHT4 External",
              3004: "Humidity - DHT4 External",
              3005: "Soil Moisture - Plant 2"
          }
     
          @dashboard_bp.route("/dashboard")
          def dashboard():
              return render_template("dashboard.html")
     
     
          @dashboard_bp.route("/api/dashboard-data")
          def dashboard_data():
              session = SessionLocal()
              try:
                  # --- RAW SENSOR DATA ---
                  raw_data = session.query(SensorData).order_by(SensorData.Timestamp).limit(100).all()
                  grouped_raw = defaultdict(list)
                  for entry in raw_data:
                      grouped_raw[entry.SensorID].append({
                          "timestamp": entry.Timestamp.isoformat(),
                          "value": entry.Value
                      })
     
                  raw_plot_data = [
                      {
                          "label": sensor_labels.get(sensor_id, f"Sensor {sensor_id}"),
                          "sensor_id": sensor_id,
                          "timestamps": [d["timestamp"] for d in data],
                          "values": [d["value"] for d in data]
                      }
                      for sensor_id, data in grouped_raw.items()
                  ]
     
                  # --- KALMAN FILTER FUSION DATA ---
                  kalman_data = session.query(KalmanFilterFusionData).order_by(KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp).limit(100).all()
                  grouped_kalman = defaultdict(list)
                  for entry in kalman_data:
                      grouped_kalman[entry.SensorID].append({
                          "timestamp": entry.Timestamp.isoformat(),
                          "value": entry.FusedValue
                      })
                  kalman_plot_data = [
                      {
                          "label": sensor_labels.get(sensor_id, f"Sensor {sensor_id}"),
                          "sensor_id": sensor_id,
                          "timestamps": [d["timestamp"] for d in data],
                          "values": [d["value"] for d in data]
                      }
                      for sensor_id, data in grouped_kalman.items()
                  ]
     
                  # --- WEIGHTED AVERAGE FUSION DATA ---
                  weighted_data = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData).order_by(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp).limit(100).all()
                  grouped_weighted = defaultdict(list)
                  for entry in weighted_data:
                      grouped_weighted[entry.SensorType].append({
                          "timestamp": entry.Timestamp.isoformat(),
                          "value": entry.FusedValue
                      })
                  weighted_plot_data = [
                      {
                          "sensor_type": sensor_type,
                          "timestamps": [d["timestamp"] for d in data],
                          "values": [d["value"] for d in data]
                      }
                      for sensor_type, data in grouped_weighted.items()
                  ]
     
                  return jsonify({
                      "raw": raw_plot_data,
                      "kalman": kalman_plot_data,
                      "weighted": weighted_plot_data
                  })
     
              finally:
                  session.close()
          â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘
     
     â”œâ”€â”€ data_retrival.py
          â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
          from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker
          from database_setup import engine, Actuator, UserInteraction
          import pandas as pd
     
          # Create session
          Session = sessionmaker(bind=engine)
          session = Session()
     
          # === Fetch last row from Actuator table ===
          last_actuator = (
              session.query(Actuator)
              .order_by(Actuator.LastUpdated.desc())
              .first()
          )
     
          # Convert to dict
          actuator_data = {
              "ActuatorID": last_actuator.ActuatorID,
              "ActuatorName": last_actuator.ActuatorName,
              "Status": last_actuator.Status,
              "LastUpdated": last_actuator.LastUpdated,
              "UserID": last_actuator.UserID,
              "DeviceID": last_actuator.DeviceID
          } if last_actuator else {}
     
          # === Fetch last row from UserInteraction table ===
          last_interaction = (
              session.query(UserInteraction)
              .order_by(UserInteraction.Timestamp.desc())
              .first()
          )
     
          # Convert to dict
          interaction_data = {
              "InteractionID": last_interaction.InteractionID,
              "UserID": last_interaction.UserID,
              "DeviceID": last_interaction.DeviceID,
              "ActuatorID": last_interaction.ActuatorID,
              "Action": last_interaction.Action,
              "Timestamp": last_interaction.Timestamp
          } if last_interaction else {}
     
          # Close session
          session.close()
     
          # Print output
          print("\n=== Last Actuator Entry ===")
          print(pd.DataFrame([actuator_data]))
     
          print("\n=== Last UserInteraction Entry ===")
          print(pd.DataFrame([interaction_data]))
          â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

     â”‚        #  Example: Insert multiple temperature readings at once
     â”‚        sensor_readings = [
     â”‚            {"DeviceID": 1, "SensorType": "humidity", "Value": 21.2},

     â”‚            {"DeviceID": 3, "SensorType": "humidity", "Value": 23.4},
     â”‚            {"DeviceID": 4, "SensorType": "humidity", "Value": 24.4},

     â”‚        ]

     â”‚        import random
     â”‚        from datetime import datetime, timedelta
     â”‚        from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     â”‚        from faker import Faker
     â”‚        from database_setup import (
     â”‚            Base, engine, SessionLocal,
     â”‚            UserCredentials, Device, Sensor,
     â”‚            SensorData, KalmanFilterFusionData,
     â”‚            Actuator
     â”‚        )
     â”‚
     â”‚        fake = Faker()
     â”‚
     â”‚        # Use same sensor IDs from your fusion logic
     â”‚        TEMP_SENSOR_IDS = [2099, 2092, 3093]
     â”‚        HUM_SENSOR_IDS = [2091, 2034, 3027]
     â”‚        ALL_SENSOR_IDS = TEMP_SENSOR_IDS + HUM_SENSOR_IDS
     â”‚
     â”‚        def create_dummy_user(session: Session):
     â”‚            user = UserCredentials(
     â”‚                Username="test_user",
     â”‚                PasswordHash="hashed_password",
     â”‚                Email="test@example.com",
     â”‚                FullName="Test User"
     â”‚            )
     â”‚            session.add(user)
     â”‚            session.flush()  # get UserID for foreign keys
     â”‚            return user
     â”‚
     â”‚        def create_dummy_devices(session: Session):
     â”‚            devices = []
     â”‚            for i in range(1, 4):
     â”‚                device = Device(
     â”‚                    DeviceID=1000 + i,
     â”‚                    DeviceName=f"Device_{i}",
     â”‚                    Location=fake.city()
     â”‚                )
     â”‚                session.add(device)
     â”‚                devices.append(device)
     â”‚            session.flush()
     â”‚            return devices
     â”‚
     â”‚        def create_dummy_sensors(session: Session, devices):
     â”‚            sensors = []
     â”‚            sensor_definitions = [
     â”‚                (TEMP_SENSOR_IDS[0], devices[0], "Temperature"),
     â”‚                (TEMP_SENSOR_IDS[1], devices[1], "Temperature"),
     â”‚                (TEMP_SENSOR_IDS[2], devices[2], "Temperature"),
     â”‚                (HUM_SENSOR_IDS[0], devices[0], "Humidity"),
     â”‚                (HUM_SENSOR_IDS[1], devices[1], "Humidity"),
     â”‚                (HUM_SENSOR_IDS[2], devices[2], "Humidity"),
     â”‚            ]
     â”‚            for sensor_id, device, sensor_type in sensor_definitions:
     â”‚                sensor = Sensor(
     â”‚                    SensorID=sensor_id,
     â”‚                    DeviceID=device.DeviceID,
     â”‚                    SensorType=sensor_type,
     â”‚                    Location=device.Location
     â”‚                )
     â”‚                session.add(sensor)
     â”‚                sensors.append(sensor)
     â”‚            session.flush()
     â”‚            return sensors
     â”‚
     â”‚        def insert_sensor_data(session: Session, sensors):
     â”‚            now = datetime.utcnow()
     â”‚            for sensor in sensors:
     â”‚                for i in range(3):  # 3 entries per sensor
     â”‚                    timestamp = now - timedelta(minutes=i)
     â”‚                    value = round(random.uniform(20.0, 35.0), 2) if "Temp" in sensor.SensorType else round(random.uniform(30.0, 80.0), 2)
     â”‚
     â”‚                    # Raw sensor data
     â”‚                    sensor_data = SensorData(
     â”‚                        SensorID=sensor.SensorID,
     â”‚                        Timestamp=timestamp,
     â”‚                        Value=value
     â”‚                    )
     â”‚                    session.add(sensor_data)
     â”‚
     â”‚                    # Simulated Kalman output (slightly smoothed)
     â”‚                    kalman_value = round(value + random.uniform(-1.0, 1.0), 2)
     â”‚                    kalman_data = KalmanFilterFusionData(
     â”‚                        SensorID=sensor.SensorID,
     â”‚                        Timestamp=timestamp,
     â”‚                        FusedValue=kalman_value
     â”‚                    )
     â”‚                    session.add(kalman_data)
     â”‚
     â”‚        def create_dummy_actuators(session: Session, user, devices):
     â”‚            for i, device in enumerate(devices):
     â”‚                actuator = Actuator(
     â”‚                    ActuatorName=f"Pump_{i+1}",
     â”‚                    Status="Active" if i % 2 == 0 else "Inactive",
     â”‚                    UserID=user.UserID,
     â”‚                    DeviceID=device.DeviceID
     â”‚                )
     â”‚                session.add(actuator)
     â”‚
     â”‚        def main():
     â”‚            Base.metadata.create_all(engine)
     â”‚            session = SessionLocal()
     â”‚
     â”‚            try:
     â”‚                print("[INFO] Populating database with dummy data...")
     â”‚
     â”‚                user = create_dummy_user(session)
     â”‚                devices = create_dummy_devices(session)
     â”‚                sensors = create_dummy_sensors(session, devices)
     â”‚                insert_sensor_data(session, sensors)
     â”‚                create_dummy_actuators(session, user, devices)
     â”‚
     â”‚                session.commit()
     â”‚                print("[SUCCESS] Database populated successfully.")
     â”‚
     â”‚            except Exception as e:
     â”‚                session.rollback()
     â”‚                print(f"[ERROR] Failed to populate database: {e}")
     â”‚            finally:
     â”‚                session.close()
     â”‚
     â”‚        if __name__ == "__main__":
     â”‚            main()
