     â”‚        â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ database_setup.py
     â”‚        â”‚        â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     â”‚        â”‚        from sqlalchemy import create_engine, Column, Integer, Float, String, DateTime, ForeignKey
     â”‚        â”‚        from sqlalchemy.orm import relationship, sessionmaker, DeclarativeBase
     â”‚        â”‚        from datetime import datetime
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Database connection
     â”‚        â”‚        DATABASE_URL = "sqlite:///greenhouse.db"
     â”‚        â”‚        engine = create_engine(DATABASE_URL, echo=True)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Create session factory
     â”‚        â”‚        SessionLocal = sessionmaker(bind=engine)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        #  Base Model
     â”‚        â”‚        class Base(DeclarativeBase):
     â”‚        â”‚            pass
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        #  Devices Table
     â”‚        â”‚        class Device(Base):
     â”‚        â”‚            __tablename__ = "devices"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            DeviceID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
     â”‚        â”‚            DeviceName = Column(String(50), nullable=False)
     â”‚        â”‚            Location = Column(String(100))
     â”‚        â”‚            Status = Column(String(20))  # e.g., "Active", "Inactive"
     â”‚        â”‚            Type = Column(String(50))  # e.g., "ESP32", "Raspberry Pi"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            sensor_data = relationship("SensorData", back_populates="device")
     â”‚        â”‚            user_interactions = relationship("UserInteraction", back_populates="device")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        #  SensorData Table
     â”‚        â”‚        class SensorData(Base):
     â”‚        â”‚            __tablename__ = "sensor_data"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            DataID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
     â”‚        â”‚            DeviceID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("devices.DeviceID"))
     â”‚        â”‚            Timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
     â”‚        â”‚            SensorType = Column(String(50))  # e.g., "temperature", "humidity"
     â”‚        â”‚            Value = Column(Float)  # Sensor reading value
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            device = relationship("Device", back_populates="sensor_data")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        #  UserInteractions Table
     â”‚        â”‚        class UserInteraction(Base):
     â”‚        â”‚            __tablename__ = "user_interactions"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            InteractionID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
     â”‚        â”‚            UserID = Column(Integer)  # Assuming users are stored elsewhere
     â”‚        â”‚            DeviceID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("devices.DeviceID"))
     â”‚        â”‚            Action = Column(String(20), nullable=False)  # e.g., "Turn On", "Turn Off"
     â”‚        â”‚            Timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            device = relationship("Device", back_populates="user_interactions")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        #  Create Tables in SQLite
     â”‚        â”‚        Base.metadata.create_all(engine)
     â”‚        â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘
     â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ database_setups.py
     â”‚        â”‚        â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     â”‚        â”‚        from sqlalchemy import (
     â”‚        â”‚            create_engine, Column, Integer, Float, String, DateTime, ForeignKey
     â”‚        â”‚        )
     â”‚        â”‚        from sqlalchemy.orm import relationship, sessionmaker, DeclarativeBase
     â”‚        â”‚        from datetime import datetime
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Database connection
     â”‚        â”‚        DATABASE_URL = "sqlite:///greenhouse.db"
     â”‚        â”‚        engine = create_engine(DATABASE_URL, echo=True)
     â”‚        â”‚        SessionLocal = sessionmaker(bind=engine)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Base class
     â”‚        â”‚        class Base(DeclarativeBase):
     â”‚        â”‚            pass
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Devices Table
     â”‚        â”‚        class Device(Base):
     â”‚        â”‚            __tablename__ = "devices"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            DeviceID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
     â”‚        â”‚            DeviceName = Column(String(50), nullable=False)
     â”‚        â”‚            Location = Column(String(100))
     â”‚        â”‚            Status = Column(String(20))  # e.g., "Active", "Inactive"
     â”‚        â”‚            Type = Column(String(50))    # e.g., "ESP32", "Raspberry Pi"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            # Relationships
     â”‚        â”‚            sensors = relationship("Sensor", back_populates="device", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
     â”‚        â”‚            sensor_data = relationship("SensorData", secondary="sensors", viewonly=True)
     â”‚        â”‚            user_interactions = relationship("UserInteraction", back_populates="device", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
     â”‚        â”‚            kalman_fusions = relationship("KalmanFilterFusionData", back_populates="device", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
     â”‚        â”‚            weighted_fusions = relationship("WeightedAverageFusionData", back_populates="device", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Sensors Table
     â”‚        â”‚        class Sensor(Base):
     â”‚        â”‚            __tablename__ = "sensors"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            SensorID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
     â”‚        â”‚            DeviceID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("devices.DeviceID"), nullable=False)
     â”‚        â”‚            SensorType = Column(String(50))  # e.g., "DHT", "SoilMoisture"
     â”‚        â”‚            SensorIndex = Column(Integer)    # To distinguish multiple sensors of same type
     â”‚        â”‚            Location = Column(String(100))   # e.g., "Top Left"
     â”‚        â”‚            Status = Column(String(20), default="Active")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            device = relationship("Device", back_populates="sensors")
     â”‚        â”‚            sensor_data = relationship("SensorData", back_populates="sensor", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # SensorData Table
     â”‚        â”‚        class SensorData(Base):
     â”‚        â”‚            __tablename__ = "sensor_data"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            DataID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
     â”‚        â”‚            SensorID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("sensors.SensorID"), nullable=False)
     â”‚        â”‚            Timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
     â”‚        â”‚            Value = Column(Float, nullable=False)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            sensor = relationship("Sensor", back_populates="sensor_data")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # UserInteractions Table
     â”‚        â”‚        class UserInteraction(Base):
     â”‚        â”‚            __tablename__ = "user_interactions"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            InteractionID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
     â”‚        â”‚            UserID = Column(Integer)
     â”‚        â”‚            DeviceID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("devices.DeviceID"), nullable=False)
     â”‚        â”‚            ActuatorID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("actuators.ActuatorID"))  # Optional, if interaction is with an actuator
     â”‚        â”‚            Action = Column(String(20), nullable=False)  # e.g., "Turn On", "Turn Off"
     â”‚        â”‚            Timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            device = relationship("Device", back_populates="user_interactions")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Kalman Filter Fusion Table
     â”‚        â”‚        class KalmanFilterFusionData(Base):
     â”‚        â”‚            __tablename__ = "kalman_filter_fusion"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            FusionID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
     â”‚        â”‚            SensorID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("kalmanFilterFusionData.SensorID"), nullable=False)
     â”‚        â”‚            Timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
     â”‚        â”‚            FusedValue = Column(Float, nullable=False)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            sensor = relationship("Sensor", back_populates="kalmanFilterFusionData"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Weighted Average Fusion Table
     â”‚        â”‚        class WeightedAverageFusionData(Base):
     â”‚        â”‚            __tablename__ = "weighted_average_fusion"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            FusionID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
     â”‚        â”‚            DeviceID = Column(Integer, ForeignKey("devices.DeviceID"), nullable=False)
     â”‚        â”‚            SensorType = Column(String(50))  # Optional
     â”‚        â”‚            Timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
     â”‚        â”‚            FusedValue = Column(Float, nullable=False)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            device = relationship("Device", back_populates="weighted_fusions")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Actuators Table
     â”‚        â”‚        class Actuator(Base):
     â”‚        â”‚            __tablename__ = "actuators"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            ActuatorID = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
     â”‚        â”‚            ActuatorName = Column(String(50), nullable=False, unique=True)
     â”‚        â”‚            Status = Column(String(20), nullable=False)  # e.g., "On", "Off"
     â”‚        â”‚            LastUpdated = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
     â”‚        â”‚            UserID = Column(Integer)  # Refers to the user who last updated it
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            def __repr__(self):
     â”‚        â”‚                return f"<Actuator(Name={self.ActuatorName}, Status={self.Status})>"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Create all tables
     â”‚        â”‚        Base.metadata.create_all(engine)
     â”‚        â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘
     â”‚

     â”‚        â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ network.py
     â”‚        â”‚        â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     â”‚        â”‚        from flask import request, jsonify
     â”‚        â”‚        from database_setup import SessionLocal, SensorData, Device,UserInteraction
     â”‚        â”‚        from datetime import datetime
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Device (Microcontrollers) authentication credentials for sending sensor data to the server
     â”‚        â”‚        credentials = {
     â”‚        â”‚            "esp_Temp_humid_1": "esp_password",
     â”‚        â”‚            "esp_Soil_moisture_1": "esp_password"
     â”‚        â”‚        }
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def action_based_on_sensor(DeviceName, temperature=0, humidity=0, soil_moisture=0):
     â”‚        â”‚            session = SessionLocal()
     â”‚        â”‚            try:
     â”‚        â”‚                if DeviceName == "esp_Temp_humid_1" and temperature > 30:
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.add(UserInteraction(DeviceID=11, UserID=5000, Action="blink_led", Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.commit()
     â”‚        â”‚                    return "blink_led"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                elif DeviceName == "esp_Soil_moisture_1" and soil_moisture > 30:
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.add(UserInteraction(DeviceID=12, UserID=5000, Action="blink_led", Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.commit()
     â”‚        â”‚                    return "blink_led"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                return "no_action"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            finally:
     â”‚        â”‚                session.close()
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def store_sensor_data(device_id, DeviceName, temperature=None, humidity=None, soil_moisture=None):
     â”‚        â”‚            session = SessionLocal()
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            # Ensure device exists in the database
     â”‚        â”‚            device = session.query(Device).filter_by(DeviceID=device_id).first()
     â”‚        â”‚            if not device:
     â”‚        â”‚                device = Device(DeviceID=device_id, DeviceName=DeviceName, Type="ESP32", Location="Unknown", Status="Active")
     â”‚        â”‚                session.add(device)
     â”‚        â”‚                session.commit()
     â”‚        â”‚                session.refresh(device)  # Ensure we have the latest DeviceID
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            # Store sensor readings for the specific device ID received from ESP
     â”‚        â”‚            if temperature is not None and device_id in {1, 2, 3}:
     â”‚        â”‚                session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="temperature", Value=temperature, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            if humidity is not None and device_id in {4, 5, 6}:
     â”‚        â”‚                session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="humidity", Value=humidity, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            if soil_moisture is not None and device_id in {7, 8}:
     â”‚        â”‚                session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="soil_moisture", Value=soil_moisture, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            session.commit()
     â”‚        â”‚            session.close()
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def receive_sensor_data(request):
     â”‚        â”‚            # Get Authorization header
     â”‚        â”‚            auth = request.authorization
     â”‚        â”‚            if not auth or credentials.get(auth.username) != auth.password:
     â”‚        â”‚                return jsonify({"error": "Unauthorized"}), 401
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            try:
     â”‚        â”‚                data = request.json
     â”‚        â”‚                if not data:
     â”‚        â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Invalid or missing JSON payload"}), 400
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                device_id = data.get('DeviceID')  # This is an integer
     â”‚        â”‚                DeviceName = data.get('DeviceName')  # This is a string
     â”‚        â”‚                temperature = data.get('temperature')
     â”‚        â”‚                humidity = data.get('humidity')
     â”‚        â”‚                soil_moisture = data.get('soil_moisture')  # Fixed key
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                if not device_id or not DeviceName:
     â”‚        â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Missing 'DeviceID' or 'DeviceName' in payload"}), 400
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                print(f"Received JSON payload: {data}")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                # Store the data in the database
     â”‚        â”‚                store_sensor_data(device_id, DeviceName, temperature, humidity, soil_moisture)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                # Determine action based on sensor data
     â”‚        â”‚                action = action_based_on_sensor(DeviceName, temperature, humidity, soil_moisture)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                response = {"DeviceName": DeviceName, "action": action}
     â”‚        â”‚                return jsonify(response)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            except Exception as e:
     â”‚        â”‚                print(f"Error processing request: {e}")
     â”‚        â”‚                return jsonify({"error": "Internal Server Error"}), 500
     â”‚        â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘
     â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ newer_network.py
     â”‚        â”‚        â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     â”‚        â”‚        from flask import request, jsonify
     â”‚        â”‚        import time
     â”‚        â”‚        from sqlalchemy import desc
     â”‚        â”‚        from datetime import datetime
     â”‚        â”‚        from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     â”‚        â”‚        from database_setup import (
     â”‚        â”‚            SessionLocal, SensorData, Sensor, Device, UserInteraction,
     â”‚        â”‚            Actuator, WeightedAverageFusionData, KalmanFilterFusionData
     â”‚        â”‚        )
     â”‚        â”‚        from weightedAverage import process_weighted_fusion
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Authentication credentials for devices
     â”‚        â”‚        credentials = {
     â”‚        â”‚            "Ventilation_System_ESP": "password",
     â”‚        â”‚            "Irrigation_System_ESP": "password",
     â”‚        â”‚            "web_control": "web_password"
     â”‚        â”‚        }
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Constants
     â”‚        â”‚        DEFAULT_USER_ID = 5000  # Server user
     â”‚        â”‚        TEMP_THRESHOLD = 30
     â”‚        â”‚        HUM_THRESHOLD = 40
     â”‚        â”‚        SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD = 30
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        TEMP_SENSOR_IDS = [2099, 2092, 3093]
     â”‚        â”‚        HUM_SENSOR_IDS = [2091, 2034, 3027]
     â”‚        â”‚        WEIGHTS = [0.5, 0.3, 0.2]
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Actuator Names
     â”‚        â”‚        INTAKE_SHUTTER = "intake_shutter"
     â”‚        â”‚        WATER_PUMP = "water_pump"
     â”‚        â”‚        VENTILATION_FAN = "ventilation_fan"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Device IDs
     â”‚        â”‚        Ventilation_System_ESP_ID = 2000
     â”‚        â”‚        Irrigation_System_ESP_ID = 3000
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        soil_sensor_1id = 2005
     â”‚        â”‚        soil_sensor_2id = 3002
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def get_fused_values_by_sensors(session: Session, *sensor_ids: int):
     â”‚        â”‚            fused_values = {}
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            if not sensor_ids:
     â”‚        â”‚                return fused_values  # No IDs provided â†’ return empty
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            for sensor_id in sensor_ids:
     â”‚        â”‚                if sensor_id is None:
     â”‚        â”‚                    continue
     â”‚        â”‚                fusion = (
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.query(KalmanFilterFusionData)
     â”‚        â”‚                    .filter_by(SensorID=sensor_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                    .order_by(desc(KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp))
     â”‚        â”‚                    .first()
     â”‚        â”‚                )
     â”‚        â”‚                if fusion:
     â”‚        â”‚                    fused_values[sensor_id] = fusion.FusedValue
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            return fused_values
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def log_user_action(session, device_id, action, user_id, actuator_id):
     â”‚        â”‚            session.add(UserInteraction(
     â”‚        â”‚                DeviceID=device_id,
     â”‚        â”‚                Action=action,
     â”‚        â”‚                UserID=user_id,
     â”‚        â”‚                ActuatorID=actuator_id,
     â”‚        â”‚                Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()
     â”‚        â”‚            ))
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def control_actuator(session, actuator_name, status, user_id):
     â”‚        â”‚            actuator = session.query(Actuator).filter_by(ActuatorName=actuator_name).first()
     â”‚        â”‚            if not actuator:
     â”‚        â”‚                actuator = Actuator(
     â”‚        â”‚                    ActuatorName=actuator_name,
     â”‚        â”‚                    Status=status,
     â”‚        â”‚                    LastUpdated=datetime.utcnow(),
     â”‚        â”‚                    UserID=user_id
     â”‚        â”‚                )
     â”‚        â”‚                session.add(actuator)
     â”‚        â”‚            else:
     â”‚        â”‚                if actuator.Status != status:
     â”‚        â”‚                    actuator.Status = status
     â”‚        â”‚                    actuator.LastUpdated = datetime.utcnow()
     â”‚        â”‚                    actuator.UserID = user_id
     â”‚        â”‚                    log_user_action(
     â”‚        â”‚                        session,
     â”‚        â”‚                        device_id=actuator.ActuatorID,
     â”‚        â”‚                        action=f"{actuator_name}_{status.lower()}",
     â”‚        â”‚                        user_id=user_id,
     â”‚        â”‚                        actuator_id=actuator.ActuatorID
     â”‚        â”‚                    )
     â”‚        â”‚            session.commit()
     â”‚        â”‚            return actuator
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def get_latest_fused_temperature_humidity(session):
     â”‚        â”‚            latest_temp = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData).filter_by(
     â”‚        â”‚                SensorType="temperature").order_by(desc(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp)).first()
     â”‚        â”‚            latest_hum = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData).filter_by(
     â”‚        â”‚                SensorType="humidity").order_by(desc(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp)).first()
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            return {
     â”‚        â”‚                "temperature": latest_temp.FusedValue if latest_temp else None,
     â”‚        â”‚                "humidity": latest_hum.FusedValue if latest_hum else None
     â”‚        â”‚            }
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def action_based_on_sensor(user_id=DEFAULT_USER_ID):
     â”‚        â”‚            with SessionLocal() as session:
     â”‚        â”‚                result = get_fused_values_by_sensors(session, soil_sensor_1id, soil_sensor_2id)
     â”‚        â”‚                soil1 = result.get(soil_sensor_1id)
     â”‚        â”‚                soil2 = result.get(soil_sensor_2id)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                soil_moisture = None
     â”‚        â”‚                if soil1 is not None and soil2 is not None:
     â”‚        â”‚                    average = (soil1 + soil2) / 2
     â”‚        â”‚                    if 0 <= average <= 100:
     â”‚        â”‚                        soil_moisture = average
     â”‚        â”‚                elif soil1 is not None:
     â”‚        â”‚                    if 0 <= soil1 <= 100:
     â”‚        â”‚                        soil_moisture = soil1
     â”‚        â”‚                elif soil2 is not None:
     â”‚        â”‚                    if 0 <= soil2 <= 100:
     â”‚        â”‚                        soil_moisture = soil2
     â”‚        â”‚                # Else â†’ soil_moisture stays None
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                temperature=process_weighted_fusion(sensor_ids=TEMP_SENSOR_IDS, weights=WEIGHTS, sensor_type="Temperature")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                # Call for humidity
     â”‚        â”‚                humidity=process_weighted_fusion(sensor_ids=HUM_SENSOR_IDS, weights=WEIGHTS, sensor_type="Humidity")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                actions = []
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                try:
     â”‚        â”‚                    if temperature is not None and humidity is not None:
     â”‚        â”‚                        if temperature > TEMP_THRESHOLD or humidity > HUM_THRESHOLD:
     â”‚        â”‚                            control_actuator(session, VENTILATION_FAN, "on", user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                            control_actuator(session, INTAKE_SHUTTER, "on", user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                            actions.append("Ventilation_ON")
     â”‚        â”‚                        elif temperature < TEMP_THRESHOLD and humidity < HUM_THRESHOLD:
     â”‚        â”‚                            control_actuator(session, VENTILATION_FAN, "off", user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                            control_actuator(session, INTAKE_SHUTTER, "off", user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                            actions.append("Ventilation_OFF")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                    if soil_moisture is not None:
     â”‚        â”‚                        if soil_moisture < SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD:
     â”‚        â”‚                            control_actuator(session, WATER_PUMP, "on", user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                            actions.append("Irrigation_ON")
     â”‚        â”‚                        else:
     â”‚        â”‚                            control_actuator(session, WATER_PUMP, "off", user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                            actions.append("Irrigation_OFF")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.commit()
     â”‚        â”‚                    return ", ".join(actions) if actions else "none"
     â”‚        â”‚                except Exception as e:
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.rollback()
     â”‚        â”‚                    print(f"[ERROR] Failed to perform action: {e}")
     â”‚        â”‚                    return "error"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def get_or_create_device(session, device_id, device_name):
     â”‚        â”‚            device = session.query(Device).filter_by(DeviceID=device_id).first()
     â”‚        â”‚            if not device:
     â”‚        â”‚                device = Device(DeviceID=device_id, DeviceName=device_name, Location="Unknown", Status="Active")
     â”‚        â”‚                session.add(device)
     â”‚        â”‚                session.commit()
     â”‚        â”‚                session.refresh(device)
     â”‚        â”‚            return device
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def get_or_create_sensor(session,sensor_id, device_id, sensor_type):
     â”‚        â”‚            sensor = session.query(Sensor).filter_by(SensorID=sensor_id, SensorType=sensor_type).first()
     â”‚        â”‚            if not sensor:
     â”‚        â”‚                sensor = Sensor(SensorID=sensor_id, DeviceID=device_id, SensorType=sensor_type, Location="Unknown", Status="Active")
     â”‚        â”‚                session.add(sensor)
     â”‚        â”‚                session.commit()
     â”‚        â”‚                session.refresh(sensor)
     â”‚        â”‚            return sensor
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def store_sensor_value(session, sensor, value):
     â”‚        â”‚            session.add(SensorData(SensorID=sensor.SensorID, Value=value, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def store_sensor_data(device_id, device_name,sensor_id,
     â”‚        â”‚                              temperature=None, filtered_temperature=None,
     â”‚        â”‚                              humidity=None, filtered_humidity=None,
     â”‚        â”‚                              soil_moisture=None, filtered_soil_moisture=None):
     â”‚        â”‚            with SessionLocal() as session:
     â”‚        â”‚                try:
     â”‚        â”‚                    get_or_create_device(session, device_id, device_name)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                    if temperature is not None:
     â”‚        â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "temperature")
     â”‚        â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, temperature)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                    if filtered_temperature is not None:
     â”‚        â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "temperature_filtered")
     â”‚        â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, filtered_temperature)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                    if humidity is not None:
     â”‚        â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "humidity")
     â”‚        â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, humidity)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                    if filtered_humidity is not None:
     â”‚        â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "humidity_filtered")
     â”‚        â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, filtered_humidity)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                    if soil_moisture is not None:
     â”‚        â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "soil_moisture")
     â”‚        â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, soil_moisture)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                    if filtered_soil_moisture is not None:
     â”‚        â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "soil_moisture_filtered")
     â”‚        â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, filtered_soil_moisture)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.commit()
     â”‚        â”‚                except Exception as e:
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.rollback()
     â”‚        â”‚                    print(f"[ERROR] Failed to store sensor data: {e}")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def receive_sensor_data(request):
     â”‚        â”‚            auth = request.authorization
     â”‚        â”‚            if not auth or credentials.get(auth.username) != auth.password:
     â”‚        â”‚                return jsonify({"error": "Unauthorized"}), 401
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            try:
     â”‚        â”‚                data = request.get_json()
     â”‚        â”‚                if not data:
     â”‚        â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Invalid or missing JSON payload"}), 400
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                device_id = data.get('DeviceID')
     â”‚        â”‚                device_name = data.get('DeviceName')
     â”‚        â”‚                sensor_id = data.get('SensorID')
     â”‚        â”‚                if not device_id or not device_name:
     â”‚        â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Missing DeviceID or DeviceName"}), 400
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                temperature = data.get('temperature')
     â”‚        â”‚                filtered_temperature = data.get('filtered_temperature')
     â”‚        â”‚                humidity = data.get('humidity')
     â”‚        â”‚                filtered_humidity = data.get('filtered_humidity')
     â”‚        â”‚                soil_moisture = data.get('soil_moisture')
     â”‚        â”‚                filtered_soil_moisture = data.get('filtered_soil_moisture')
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                store_sensor_data(device_id, device_name,sensor_id,
     â”‚        â”‚                                  temperature, filtered_temperature,
     â”‚        â”‚                                  humidity, filtered_humidity,
     â”‚        â”‚                                  soil_moisture, filtered_soil_moisture)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                print(f"[INFO] Received data from DeviceID: {device_id}, SensorID: {sensor_id}")
     â”‚        â”‚                # Optional: wait for fusion update to complete if it's not sync
     â”‚        â”‚                time.sleep(5)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                action_result = action_based_on_sensor()
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                with SessionLocal() as session:
     â”‚        â”‚                    latest = get_latest_fused_temperature_humidity(session)
     â”‚        â”‚                    soil_data = get_fused_values_by_sensors(session, soil_sensor_1id, soil_sensor_2id)
     â”‚        â”‚                    avg_soil = None
     â”‚        â”‚                    if soil_data:
     â”‚        â”‚                        values = list(soil_data.values())
     â”‚        â”‚                        avg_soil = sum(values) / len(values) if values else None
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                return jsonify({
     â”‚        â”‚                    "status": "success",
     â”‚        â”‚                    "action": action_result,
     â”‚        â”‚                    "temperature": latest["temperature"],
     â”‚        â”‚                    "humidity": latest["humidity"],
     â”‚        â”‚                    "soil_moisture": avg_soil
     â”‚        â”‚                }), 200
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            except Exception as e:
     â”‚        â”‚                print(f"[ERROR] Failed to receive/process sensor data: {e}")
     â”‚        â”‚                return jsonify({"error": "Internal Server Error"}), 500
     â”‚        â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘
     â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚   â””â”€â”€ old_network.py
     â”‚        â”‚        â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     â”‚        â”‚        from flask import request, jsonify
     â”‚        â”‚        from webdevelopment.database_setup import SessionLocal, SensorData, Device, UserInteraction, Actuator, WeightedAverageFusionData
     â”‚        â”‚        from datetime import datetime
     â”‚        â”‚        from webdevelopment.weightedAverage import process_weighted_fusion
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Authentication credentials for devices
     â”‚        â”‚        credentials = {
     â”‚        â”‚            "Ventilation_System_ESP ": "password",
     â”‚        â”‚            "Irrigation_System_ESP": "password"
     â”‚        â”‚        }
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Constants
     â”‚        â”‚        DEFAULT_USER_ID = 5000  # Server user
     â”‚        â”‚        TEMP_THRESHOLD = 30
     â”‚        â”‚        HUM_THRESHOLD = 40
     â”‚        â”‚        SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD = 30
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Actuator Names
     â”‚        â”‚        INTAKE_SHUTTER = "intake_shutter"
     â”‚        â”‚        WATER_PUMP = "water_pump"
     â”‚        â”‚        VENTILATION_FAN = "ventilation_fan"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        # Device Names
     â”‚        â”‚        Ventilation_System_ESP = 1111
     â”‚        â”‚        Irrigation_System_ESP = 2222
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def log_user_action(session, device_id, action, user_id):
     â”‚        â”‚            interaction = UserInteraction(
     â”‚        â”‚                DeviceID=device_id,
     â”‚        â”‚                Action=action,
     â”‚        â”‚                UserID=user_id,
     â”‚        â”‚                Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()
     â”‚        â”‚            )
     â”‚        â”‚            session.add(interaction)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def control_actuator(session, actuator_name, status, user_id):
     â”‚        â”‚            actuator = session.query(Actuator).filter_by(ActuatorName=actuator_name).first()
     â”‚        â”‚            if not actuator:
     â”‚        â”‚                actuator = Actuator(ActuatorName=actuator_name, Status=status, LastUpdated=datetime.utcnow(), UserID=user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                session.add(actuator)
     â”‚        â”‚            else:
     â”‚        â”‚                actuator.Status = status
     â”‚        â”‚                actuator.LastUpdated = datetime.utcnow()
     â”‚        â”‚                actuator.UserID = user_id
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            # Log who triggered this actuator
     â”‚        â”‚            log_user_action(session, device_id=actuator.ActuatorID, action=f"{actuator_name}_{status.lower()}", user_id=user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚            return True
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def action_based_on_sensor(DeviceName, temperature=0, humidity=0, soil_moisture=0, user_id=DEFAULT_USER_ID):
     â”‚        â”‚            session = SessionLocal()
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            try:
     â”‚        â”‚                if  temperature > TEMP_THRESHOLD or humidity > HUM_THRESHOLD:
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                    control_actuator(session, VENTILATION_FAN, "On", user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                    control_actuator(session, INTAKE_SHUTTER, "On", user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                    log_user_action(session, Ventilation_System_ESP,"On", user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                    log_user_action(session, INTAKE_SHUTTER,"On", user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                    action_taken = "VENTILATION_System_on"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                elif soil_moisture < SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD:
     â”‚        â”‚                    control_actuator(session, WATER_PUMP, "On", user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                    log_user_action(session, Irrigation_System_ESP, "On", user_id)
     â”‚        â”‚                    action_taken = "Irrigation_System_on"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                session.commit()
     â”‚        â”‚                return action_taken
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            except Exception as e:
     â”‚        â”‚                session.rollback()
     â”‚        â”‚                print(f"[ERROR] Failed to perform action: {e}")
     â”‚        â”‚                return "error"
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            finally:
     â”‚        â”‚                session.close()
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def store_sensor_data(device_id, DeviceName, temperature=None, filtered_temperature=None, humidity=None, filtered_humidity=None, soil_moisture=None, filtered_soil_moisture= None):
     â”‚        â”‚            session = SessionLocal()
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            try:
     â”‚        â”‚                # Ensure device exists
     â”‚        â”‚                device = session.query(Device).filter_by(DeviceID=device_id).first()
     â”‚        â”‚                if not device:
     â”‚        â”‚                    device = Device(DeviceID=device_id, DeviceName=DeviceName, Type="ESP32", Location="Unknown", Status="Active")
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.add(device)
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.commit()
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.refresh(device)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                # Store relevant sensor data
     â”‚        â”‚                if temperature is not None and device_id in {1, 2, 3, 4}:
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="temperature", Value=temperature, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚        â”‚                if filtered_temperature is not None and device_id in {1, 2, 3, 4}:
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, FusedValue=temperature, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚        â”‚                if humidity is not None and device_id in {5, 6, 7, 8}:
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="humidity", Value=humidity, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚        â”‚                if filtered_humidity is not None and device_id in {5, 6, 7, 8}:
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, FusedValue=temperature, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚        â”‚                if soil_moisture is not None and device_id in {9,10}:
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="soil_moisture", Value=soil_moisture, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚        â”‚                if filtered_soil_moisture is not None and device_id in {9,10}:
     â”‚        â”‚                    session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, FusedValue=temperature, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚        â”‚                session.commit()
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            except Exception as e:
     â”‚        â”‚                session.rollback()
     â”‚        â”‚                print(f"[ERROR] Failed to store sensor data: {e}")
     â”‚        â”‚            finally:
     â”‚        â”‚                session.close()
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚        def receive_sensor_data(request):
     â”‚        â”‚            # Basic HTTP Auth
     â”‚        â”‚            auth = request.authorization
     â”‚        â”‚            if not auth or credentials.get(auth.username) != auth.password:
     â”‚        â”‚                return jsonify({"error": "Unauthorized"}), 401
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            try:
     â”‚        â”‚                data = request.json
     â”‚        â”‚                if not data:
     â”‚        â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Invalid or missing JSON payload"}), 400
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                DeviceID = data.get('DeviceID')
     â”‚        â”‚                DeviceName = data.get('DeviceName')
     â”‚        â”‚                temperature = data.get('temperature')
     â”‚        â”‚                filtered_temperature = data.get('filtered_temperature')
     â”‚        â”‚                humidity = data.get('humidity')
     â”‚        â”‚                filtered_humidity = data.get('filtered_humidity')
     â”‚        â”‚                soil_moisture = data.get('soil_moisture')
     â”‚        â”‚                filtered_soil_moisture = data.get('filtered_soil_moisture')
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                if not DeviceID:
     â”‚        â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Missing 'DeviceID' in payload"}), 400
     â”‚        â”‚                if not DeviceName:
     â”‚        â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Missing 'DeviceName' in payload"}), 400
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                print(f"Received payload: from {DeviceName}")
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                store_sensor_data(DeviceID, DeviceName, temperature, humidity, soil_moisture)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                process_weighted_fusion()
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                action = action_based_on_sensor(DeviceName, temperature, humidity, soil_moisture)
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                if action == "VENTILATION_System_on":
     â”‚        â”‚                    return jsonify({"DeviceName": "Ventilation_System_ESP", "action": action})
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                elif action == "Irrigation_System_on":
     â”‚        â”‚                    return jsonify({"DeviceName": "Irrigation_System_ESP", "action": action})
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                elif action == "error":
     â”‚        â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Failed to perform action"}), 500
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚                else:
     â”‚        â”‚                    return jsonify({"DeviceName": DeviceName, "action": "No action taken"}), 200
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚
     â”‚        â”‚            except Exception as e:
     â”‚        â”‚                print(f"[ERROR] Exception in receive_sensor_data: {e}")
     â”‚        â”‚                return jsonify({"error": "Internal Server Error"}), 500
     â”‚        â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

     â”‚        â”œâ”€â”€ webserver.code-workspace
     â”‚        â””â”€â”€ weightedAverage.py
     â”‚             â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     â”‚             from datetime import datetime, timedelta
     â”‚             from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     â”‚             from database_setup import KalmanFilterFusionData, WeightedAverageFusionData, SessionLocal
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚             def weighted_average_fusion(values, weights):
     â”‚                 """Perform weighted average of given values with weights."""
     â”‚                 if len(values) != len(weights):
     â”‚                     raise ValueError("Length of values and weights must match.")
     â”‚                 return sum(v * w for v, w in zip(values, weights))
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚             def fetch_recent_sensor_data(session, sensor_ids, window_seconds):
     â”‚                 """Fetch the most recent Kalman-filtered readings for given sensor_ids within time window."""
     â”‚                 now = datetime.utcnow()
     â”‚                 window_start = now - timedelta(seconds=window_seconds)
     â”‚                 latest_data = {}
     â”‚
     â”‚                 for sensor_id in sensor_ids:
     â”‚                     entry = session.query(KalmanFilterFusionData)\
     â”‚                         .filter(KalmanFilterFusionData.SensorID == sensor_id)\
     â”‚                         .filter(KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp >= window_start)\
     â”‚                         .order_by(KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp.desc())\
     â”‚                         .first()
     â”‚                     if entry:
     â”‚                         latest_data[sensor_id] = entry.FusedValue
     â”‚
     â”‚                 return latest_data
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚             def process_weighted_fusion(sensor_ids, weights, sensor_type, fusion_window_seconds=60):
     â”‚                 """
     â”‚                 Run weighted average fusion on a given set of sensor IDs and weights.
     â”‚
     â”‚                 Args:
     â”‚                     sensor_ids (list): List of sensor IDs.
     â”‚                     weights (list): Corresponding weights (same length as sensor_ids).
     â”‚                     sensor_type (str): Sensor type label (e.g., "Temperature", "Humidity").
     â”‚                     fusion_window_seconds (int): Time window in seconds to consider valid readings.
     â”‚                 """
     â”‚                 session: Session = SessionLocal()
     â”‚                 try:
     â”‚                     sensor_data = fetch_recent_sensor_data(session, sensor_ids, fusion_window_seconds)
     â”‚
     â”‚                     if not sensor_data:
     â”‚                         print(f"[{sensor_type.upper()}] No recent readings available.")
     â”‚                         return
     â”‚
     â”‚                     available_ids = list(sensor_data.keys())
     â”‚                     available_values = [sensor_data[sid] for sid in available_ids]
     â”‚
     â”‚                     # Adjust weights to match available sensors
     â”‚                     weight_map = {sid: w for sid, w in zip(sensor_ids, weights)}
     â”‚                     available_weights = [weight_map[sid] for sid in available_ids]
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚                     # Normalize weights
     â”‚                     total_weight = sum(available_weights)
     â”‚                     normalized_weights = [w / total_weight for w in available_weights]
     â”‚
     â”‚                     fused_value = weighted_average_fusion(available_values, normalized_weights)
     â”‚
     â”‚                     session.add(WeightedAverageFusionData(
     â”‚                         SensorType=sensor_type,
     â”‚                         Timestamp=datetime.utcnow(),
     â”‚                         FusedValue=fused_value
     â”‚                     ))
     â”‚                     session.commit()
     â”‚                     print(f"[{sensor_type.upper()}] Fused value: {fused_value:.2f} from {len(available_values)} sensors.")
     â”‚                 except Exception as e:
     â”‚                     session.rollback()
     â”‚                     print(f"[ERROR] Fusion failed for {sensor_type}: {e}")
     â”‚                 finally:
     â”‚                     session.close()
     â”‚             â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘
     â”‚
     â”‚        PS D:\Documents\My AAST\Term 9\Graduation Project\Greenhouse\webdevelopment>
     â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

     â”‚        from flask import request, jsonify
     â”‚        from database_setup import SessionLocal, SensorData, Device,UserInteraction
     â”‚        from datetime import datetime
     â”‚
     â”‚        # Device (Microcontrollers) authentication credentials for sending sensor data to the server
     â”‚        credentials = {
     â”‚            "esp_Temp_humid_1": "esp_password",
     â”‚            "esp_Soil_moisture_1": "esp_password"
     â”‚        }
     â”‚
     â”‚        def action_based_on_sensor(DeviceName, temperature=0, humidity=0, soil_moisture=0):
     â”‚            session = SessionLocal()
     â”‚            try:
     â”‚                if DeviceName == "esp_Temp_humid_1" and temperature > 30:
     â”‚                    session.add(UserInteraction(DeviceID=11, UserID=5000, Action="blink_led", Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚                    session.commit()
     â”‚                    return "blink_led"
     â”‚
     â”‚                elif DeviceName == "esp_Soil_moisture_1" and soil_moisture > 30:
     â”‚                    session.add(UserInteraction(DeviceID=12, UserID=5000, Action="blink_led", Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚                    session.commit()
     â”‚                    return "blink_led"
     â”‚
     â”‚                return "no_action"
     â”‚
     â”‚            finally:
     â”‚                session.close()
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚        def store_sensor_data(device_id, DeviceName, temperature=None, humidity=None, soil_moisture=None):
     â”‚            session = SessionLocal()
     â”‚
     â”‚            # Ensure device exists in the database
     â”‚            device = session.query(Device).filter_by(DeviceID=device_id).first()
     â”‚            if not device:
     â”‚                device = Device(DeviceID=device_id, DeviceName=DeviceName, Type="ESP32", Location="Unknown", Status="Active")
     â”‚                session.add(device)
     â”‚                session.commit()
     â”‚                session.refresh(device)  # Ensure we have the latest DeviceID
     â”‚
     â”‚            # Store sensor readings for the specific device ID received from ESP
     â”‚            if temperature is not None and device_id in {1, 2, 3}:
     â”‚                session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="temperature", Value=temperature, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚
     â”‚            if humidity is not None and device_id in {4, 5, 6}:
     â”‚                session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="humidity", Value=humidity, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚
     â”‚            if soil_moisture is not None and device_id in {7, 8}:
     â”‚                session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="soil_moisture", Value=soil_moisture, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚
     â”‚            session.commit()
     â”‚            session.close()
     â”‚
     â”‚        def receive_sensor_data(request):
     â”‚            # Get Authorization header
     â”‚            auth = request.authorization
     â”‚            if not auth or credentials.get(auth.username) != auth.password:
     â”‚                return jsonify({"error": "Unauthorized"}), 401
     â”‚
     â”‚            try:
     â”‚                data = request.json
     â”‚                if not data:
     â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Invalid or missing JSON payload"}), 400
     â”‚
     â”‚                device_id = data.get('DeviceID')  # This is an integer
     â”‚                DeviceName = data.get('DeviceName')  # This is a string
     â”‚                temperature = data.get('temperature')
     â”‚                humidity = data.get('humidity')
     â”‚                soil_moisture = data.get('soil_moisture')  # Fixed key
     â”‚
     â”‚                if not device_id or not DeviceName:
     â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Missing 'DeviceID' or 'DeviceName' in payload"}), 400
     â”‚
     â”‚                print(f"Received JSON payload: {data}")
     â”‚
     â”‚                # Store the data in the database
     â”‚                store_sensor_data(device_id, DeviceName, temperature, humidity, soil_moisture)
     â”‚
     â”‚                # Determine action based on sensor data
     â”‚                action = action_based_on_sensor(DeviceName, temperature, humidity, soil_moisture)
     â”‚
     â”‚                response = {"DeviceName": DeviceName, "action": action}
     â”‚                return jsonify(response)
     â”‚
     â”‚            except Exception as e:
     â”‚                print(f"Error processing request: {e}")
     â”‚                return jsonify({"error": "Internal Server Error"}), 500
     â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘
     
     â”‚   â”œâ”€â”€ newer_network.py
     â”‚        â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     â”‚        from flask import request, jsonify
     â”‚        import time
     â”‚        from sqlalchemy import desc
     â”‚        from datetime import datetime
     â”‚        from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     â”‚        from database_setup import (
     â”‚            SessionLocal, SensorData, Sensor, Device, UserInteraction,
     â”‚            Actuator, WeightedAverageFusionData, KalmanFilterFusionData
     â”‚        )
     â”‚        from weightedAverage import process_weighted_fusion
     â”‚
     â”‚        # Authentication credentials for devices
     â”‚        credentials = {
     â”‚            "Ventilation_System_ESP": "password",
     â”‚            "Irrigation_System_ESP": "password",
     â”‚            "web_control": "web_password"
     â”‚        }
     â”‚
     â”‚        # Constants
     â”‚        DEFAULT_USER_ID = 5000  # Server user
     â”‚        TEMP_THRESHOLD = 30
     â”‚        HUM_THRESHOLD = 40
     â”‚        SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD = 30
     â”‚
     â”‚        TEMP_SENSOR_IDS = [2099, 2092, 3093]
     â”‚        HUM_SENSOR_IDS = [2091, 2034, 3027]
     â”‚        WEIGHTS = [0.5, 0.3, 0.2]
     â”‚
     â”‚        # Actuator Names
     â”‚        INTAKE_SHUTTER = "intake_shutter"
     â”‚        WATER_PUMP = "water_pump"
     â”‚        VENTILATION_FAN = "ventilation_fan"
     â”‚
     â”‚        # Device IDs
     â”‚        Ventilation_System_ESP_ID = 2000
     â”‚        Irrigation_System_ESP_ID = 3000
     â”‚
     â”‚        soil_sensor_1id = 2005
     â”‚        soil_sensor_2id = 3002
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚        def get_fused_values_by_sensors(session: Session, *sensor_ids: int):
     â”‚            fused_values = {}
     â”‚
     â”‚            if not sensor_ids:
     â”‚                return fused_values  # No IDs provided â†’ return empty
     â”‚
     â”‚            for sensor_id in sensor_ids:
     â”‚                if sensor_id is None:
     â”‚                    continue
     â”‚                fusion = (
     â”‚                    session.query(KalmanFilterFusionData)
     â”‚                    .filter_by(SensorID=sensor_id)
     â”‚                    .order_by(desc(KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp))
     â”‚                    .first()
     â”‚                )
     â”‚                if fusion:
     â”‚                    fused_values[sensor_id] = fusion.FusedValue
     â”‚
     â”‚            return fused_values
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚        def log_user_action(session, device_id, action, user_id, actuator_id):
     â”‚            session.add(UserInteraction(
     â”‚                DeviceID=device_id,
     â”‚                Action=action,
     â”‚                UserID=user_id,
     â”‚                ActuatorID=actuator_id,
     â”‚                Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()
     â”‚            ))
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚        def control_actuator(session, actuator_name, status, user_id):
     â”‚            actuator = session.query(Actuator).filter_by(ActuatorName=actuator_name).first()
     â”‚            if not actuator:
     â”‚                actuator = Actuator(
     â”‚                    ActuatorName=actuator_name,
     â”‚                    Status=status,
     â”‚                    LastUpdated=datetime.utcnow(),
     â”‚                    UserID=user_id
     â”‚                )
     â”‚                session.add(actuator)
     â”‚            else:
     â”‚                if actuator.Status != status:
     â”‚                    actuator.Status = status
     â”‚                    actuator.LastUpdated = datetime.utcnow()
     â”‚                    actuator.UserID = user_id
     â”‚                    log_user_action(
     â”‚                        session,
     â”‚                        device_id=actuator.ActuatorID,
     â”‚                        action=f"{actuator_name}_{status.lower()}",
     â”‚                        user_id=user_id,
     â”‚                        actuator_id=actuator.ActuatorID
     â”‚                    )
     â”‚            session.commit()
     â”‚            return actuator
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚        def get_latest_fused_temperature_humidity(session):
     â”‚            latest_temp = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData).filter_by(
     â”‚                SensorType="temperature").order_by(desc(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp)).first()
     â”‚            latest_hum = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData).filter_by(
     â”‚                SensorType="humidity").order_by(desc(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp)).first()
     â”‚
     â”‚            return {
     â”‚                "temperature": latest_temp.FusedValue if latest_temp else None,
     â”‚                "humidity": latest_hum.FusedValue if latest_hum else None
     â”‚            }
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚        def action_based_on_sensor(user_id=DEFAULT_USER_ID):
     â”‚            with SessionLocal() as session:
     â”‚                result = get_fused_values_by_sensors(session, soil_sensor_1id, soil_sensor_2id)
     â”‚                soil1 = result.get(soil_sensor_1id)
     â”‚                soil2 = result.get(soil_sensor_2id)
     â”‚
     â”‚                soil_moisture = None
     â”‚                if soil1 is not None and soil2 is not None:
     â”‚                    average = (soil1 + soil2) / 2
     â”‚                    if 0 <= average <= 100:
     â”‚                        soil_moisture = average
     â”‚                elif soil1 is not None:
     â”‚                    if 0 <= soil1 <= 100:
     â”‚                        soil_moisture = soil1
     â”‚                elif soil2 is not None:
     â”‚                    if 0 <= soil2 <= 100:
     â”‚                        soil_moisture = soil2
     â”‚                # Else â†’ soil_moisture stays None
     â”‚
     â”‚                temperature=process_weighted_fusion(sensor_ids=TEMP_SENSOR_IDS, weights=WEIGHTS, sensor_type="Temperature")
     â”‚
     â”‚                # Call for humidity
     â”‚                humidity=process_weighted_fusion(sensor_ids=HUM_SENSOR_IDS, weights=WEIGHTS, sensor_type="Humidity")
     â”‚
     â”‚                actions = []
     â”‚
     â”‚                try:
     â”‚                    if temperature is not None and humidity is not None:
     â”‚                        if temperature > TEMP_THRESHOLD or humidity > HUM_THRESHOLD:
     â”‚                            control_actuator(session, VENTILATION_FAN, "on", user_id)
     â”‚                            control_actuator(session, INTAKE_SHUTTER, "on", user_id)
     â”‚                            actions.append("Ventilation_ON")
     â”‚                        elif temperature < TEMP_THRESHOLD and humidity < HUM_THRESHOLD:
     â”‚                            control_actuator(session, VENTILATION_FAN, "off", user_id)
     â”‚                            control_actuator(session, INTAKE_SHUTTER, "off", user_id)
     â”‚                            actions.append("Ventilation_OFF")
     â”‚
     â”‚                    if soil_moisture is not None:
     â”‚                        if soil_moisture < SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD:
     â”‚                            control_actuator(session, WATER_PUMP, "on", user_id)
     â”‚                            actions.append("Irrigation_ON")
     â”‚                        else:
     â”‚                            control_actuator(session, WATER_PUMP, "off", user_id)
     â”‚                            actions.append("Irrigation_OFF")
     â”‚
     â”‚                    session.commit()
     â”‚                    return ", ".join(actions) if actions else "none"
     â”‚                except Exception as e:
     â”‚                    session.rollback()
     â”‚                    print(f"[ERROR] Failed to perform action: {e}")
     â”‚                    return "error"
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚        def get_or_create_device(session, device_id, device_name):
     â”‚            device = session.query(Device).filter_by(DeviceID=device_id).first()
     â”‚            if not device:
     â”‚                device = Device(DeviceID=device_id, DeviceName=device_name, Location="Unknown", Status="Active")
     â”‚                session.add(device)
     â”‚                session.commit()
     â”‚                session.refresh(device)
     â”‚            return device
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚        def get_or_create_sensor(session,sensor_id, device_id, sensor_type):
     â”‚            sensor = session.query(Sensor).filter_by(SensorID=sensor_id, SensorType=sensor_type).first()
     â”‚            if not sensor:
     â”‚                sensor = Sensor(SensorID=sensor_id, DeviceID=device_id, SensorType=sensor_type, Location="Unknown", Status="Active")
     â”‚                session.add(sensor)
     â”‚                session.commit()
     â”‚                session.refresh(sensor)
     â”‚            return sensor
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚        def store_sensor_value(session, sensor, value):
     â”‚            session.add(SensorData(SensorID=sensor.SensorID, Value=value, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚        def store_sensor_data(device_id, device_name,sensor_id,
     â”‚                              temperature=None, filtered_temperature=None,
     â”‚                              humidity=None, filtered_humidity=None,
     â”‚                              soil_moisture=None, filtered_soil_moisture=None):
     â”‚            with SessionLocal() as session:
     â”‚                try:
     â”‚                    get_or_create_device(session, device_id, device_name)
     â”‚
     â”‚                    if temperature is not None:
     â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "temperature")
     â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, temperature)
     â”‚
     â”‚                    if filtered_temperature is not None:
     â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "temperature_filtered")
     â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, filtered_temperature)
     â”‚
     â”‚                    if humidity is not None:
     â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "humidity")
     â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, humidity)
     â”‚
     â”‚                    if filtered_humidity is not None:
     â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "humidity_filtered")
     â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, filtered_humidity)
     â”‚
     â”‚                    if soil_moisture is not None:
     â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "soil_moisture")
     â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, soil_moisture)
     â”‚
     â”‚                    if filtered_soil_moisture is not None:
     â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "soil_moisture_filtered")
     â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, filtered_soil_moisture)
     â”‚
     â”‚                    session.commit()
     â”‚                except Exception as e:
     â”‚                    session.rollback()
     â”‚                    print(f"[ERROR] Failed to store sensor data: {e}")
     â”‚
     â”‚
     â”‚        def receive_sensor_data(request):
     â”‚            auth = request.authorization
     â”‚            if not auth or credentials.get(auth.username) != auth.password:
     â”‚                return jsonify({"error": "Unauthorized"}), 401
     â”‚
     â”‚            try:
     â”‚                data = request.get_json()
     â”‚                if not data:
     â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Invalid or missing JSON payload"}), 400
     â”‚
     â”‚                device_id = data.get('DeviceID')
     â”‚                device_name = data.get('DeviceName')
     â”‚                sensor_id = data.get('SensorID')
     â”‚                if not device_id or not device_name:
     â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Missing DeviceID or DeviceName"}), 400
     â”‚
     â”‚                temperature = data.get('temperature')
     â”‚                filtered_temperature = data.get('filtered_temperature')
     â”‚                humidity = data.get('humidity')
     â”‚                filtered_humidity = data.get('filtered_humidity')
     â”‚                soil_moisture = data.get('soil_moisture')
     â”‚                filtered_soil_moisture = data.get('filtered_soil_moisture')
     â”‚
     â”‚                store_sensor_data(device_id, device_name,sensor_id,
     â”‚                                  temperature, filtered_temperature,
     â”‚                                  humidity, filtered_humidity,
     â”‚                                  soil_moisture, filtered_soil_moisture)
     â”‚
     â”‚                print(f"[INFO] Received data from DeviceID: {device_id}, SensorID: {sensor_id}")
     â”‚                # Optional: wait for fusion update to complete if it's not sync
     â”‚                time.sleep(5)
     â”‚
     â”‚                action_result = action_based_on_sensor()
     â”‚
     â”‚                with SessionLocal() as session:
     â”‚                    latest = get_latest_fused_temperature_humidity(session)
     â”‚                    soil_data = get_fused_values_by_sensors(session, soil_sensor_1id, soil_sensor_2id)
     â”‚                    avg_soil = None
     â”‚                    if soil_data:
     â”‚                        values = list(soil_data.values())
     â”‚                        avg_soil = sum(values) / len(values) if values else None
     â”‚
     â”‚                return jsonify({
     â”‚                    "status": "success",
     â”‚                    "action": action_result,
     â”‚                    "temperature": latest["temperature"],
     â”‚                    "humidity": latest["humidity"],
     â”‚                    "soil_moisture": avg_soil
     â”‚                }), 200
     â”‚
     â”‚            except Exception as e:
     â”‚                print(f"[ERROR] Failed to receive/process sensor data: {e}")
     â”‚                return jsonify({"error": "Internal Server Error"}), 500
     â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘
