â”‚        â”œâ”€â”€ webserver.code-workspace
â”‚        â””â”€â”€ weightedAverage.py
â”‚             â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
â”‚             from datetime import datetime, timedelta
â”‚             from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
â”‚             from database_setup import KalmanFilterFusionData, WeightedAverageFusionData, SessionLocal
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚             def weighted_average_fusion(values, weights):
â”‚                 """Perform weighted average of given values with weights."""
â”‚                 if len(values) != len(weights):
â”‚                     raise ValueError("Length of values and weights must match.")
â”‚                 return sum(v * w for v, w in zip(values, weights))
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚             def fetch_recent_sensor_data(session, sensor_ids, window_seconds):
â”‚                 """Fetch the most recent Kalman-filtered readings for given sensor_ids within time window."""
â”‚                 now = datetime.utcnow()
â”‚                 window_start = now - timedelta(seconds=window_seconds)
â”‚                 latest_data = {}
â”‚        
â”‚                 for sensor_id in sensor_ids:
â”‚                     entry = session.query(KalmanFilterFusionData)\
â”‚                         .filter(KalmanFilterFusionData.SensorID == sensor_id)\
â”‚                         .filter(KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp >= window_start)\
â”‚                         .order_by(KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp.desc())\
â”‚                         .first()
â”‚                     if entry:
â”‚                         latest_data[sensor_id] = entry.FusedValue
â”‚        
â”‚                 return latest_data
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚             def process_weighted_fusion(sensor_ids, weights, sensor_type, fusion_window_seconds=60):
â”‚                 """
â”‚                 Run weighted average fusion on a given set of sensor IDs and weights.
â”‚        
â”‚                 Args:
â”‚                     sensor_ids (list): List of sensor IDs.
â”‚                     weights (list): Corresponding weights (same length as sensor_ids).
â”‚                     sensor_type (str): Sensor type label (e.g., "Temperature", "Humidity").
â”‚                     fusion_window_seconds (int): Time window in seconds to consider valid readings.
â”‚                 """
â”‚                 session: Session = SessionLocal()
â”‚                 try:
â”‚                     sensor_data = fetch_recent_sensor_data(session, sensor_ids, fusion_window_seconds)
â”‚        
â”‚                     if not sensor_data:
â”‚                         print(f"[{sensor_type.upper()}] No recent readings available.")
â”‚                         return
â”‚        
â”‚                     available_ids = list(sensor_data.keys())
â”‚                     available_values = [sensor_data[sid] for sid in available_ids]
â”‚        
â”‚                     # Adjust weights to match available sensors
â”‚                     weight_map = {sid: w for sid, w in zip(sensor_ids, weights)}
â”‚                     available_weights = [weight_map[sid] for sid in available_ids]
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚                     # Normalize weights
â”‚                     total_weight = sum(available_weights)
â”‚                     normalized_weights = [w / total_weight for w in available_weights]
â”‚        
â”‚                     fused_value = weighted_average_fusion(available_values, normalized_weights)
â”‚        
â”‚                     session.add(WeightedAverageFusionData(
â”‚                         SensorType=sensor_type,
â”‚                         Timestamp=datetime.utcnow(),
â”‚                         FusedValue=fused_value
â”‚                     ))
â”‚                     session.commit()
â”‚                     print(f"[{sensor_type.upper()}] Fused value: {fused_value:.2f} from {len(available_values)} sensors.")
â”‚                 except Exception as e:
â”‚                     session.rollback()
â”‚                     print(f"[ERROR] Fusion failed for {sensor_type}: {e}")
â”‚                 finally:
â”‚                     session.close()
â”‚             â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘
â”‚        
â”‚        PS D:\Documents\My AAST\Term 9\Graduation Project\Greenhouse\webdevelopment>
â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

â”‚        from flask import request, jsonify

â”‚        
â”‚        # Device (Microcontrollers) authentication credentials for sending sensor data to the server
â”‚        credentials = {
â”‚            "esp_Temp_humid_1": "esp_password",
â”‚            "esp_Soil_moisture_1": "esp_password"
â”‚        }
â”‚        
â”‚        def action_based_on_sensor(DeviceName, temperature=0, humidity=0, soil_moisture=0):
â”‚            session = SessionLocal()
â”‚            try:
â”‚                if DeviceName == "esp_Temp_humid_1" and temperature > 30:
â”‚                    session.add(UserInteraction(DeviceID=11, UserID=5000, Action="blink_led", Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
â”‚                    session.commit()
â”‚                    return "blink_led"
â”‚        
â”‚                elif DeviceName == "esp_Soil_moisture_1" and soil_moisture > 30:
â”‚                    session.add(UserInteraction(DeviceID=12, UserID=5000, Action="blink_led", Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
â”‚                    session.commit()
â”‚                    return "blink_led"
â”‚        
â”‚                return "no_action"
â”‚        
â”‚            finally:
â”‚                session.close()
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚        def store_sensor_data(device_id, DeviceName, temperature=None, humidity=None, soil_moisture=None):
â”‚            session = SessionLocal()
â”‚        
â”‚            # Ensure device exists in the database
â”‚            device = session.query(Device).filter_by(DeviceID=device_id).first()
â”‚            if not device:
â”‚                device = Device(DeviceID=device_id, DeviceName=DeviceName, Type="ESP32", Location="Unknown", Status="Active")
â”‚                session.add(device)
â”‚                session.commit()
â”‚                session.refresh(device)  # Ensure we have the latest DeviceID
â”‚        
â”‚            # Store sensor readings for the specific device ID received from ESP
â”‚            if temperature is not None and device_id in {1, 2, 3}:
â”‚                session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="temperature", Value=temperature, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
â”‚        
â”‚            if humidity is not None and device_id in {4, 5, 6}:
â”‚                session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="humidity", Value=humidity, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
â”‚        
â”‚            if soil_moisture is not None and device_id in {7, 8}:
â”‚                session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="soil_moisture", Value=soil_moisture, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
â”‚        
â”‚            session.commit()
â”‚            session.close()
â”‚        
â”‚        def receive_sensor_data(request):
â”‚            # Get Authorization header
â”‚            auth = request.authorization
â”‚            if not auth or credentials.get(auth.username) != auth.password:
â”‚                return jsonify({"error": "Unauthorized"}), 401
â”‚        
â”‚            try:
â”‚                data = request.json
â”‚                if not data:
â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Invalid or missing JSON payload"}), 400
â”‚        
â”‚                device_id = data.get('DeviceID')  # This is an integer
â”‚                DeviceName = data.get('DeviceName')  # This is a string
â”‚                temperature = data.get('temperature')
â”‚                humidity = data.get('humidity')
â”‚                soil_moisture = data.get('soil_moisture')  # Fixed key
â”‚        
â”‚                if not device_id or not DeviceName:
â”‚                    return jsonify({"error": "Missing 'DeviceID' or 'DeviceName' in payload"}), 400
â”‚        
â”‚                print(f"Received JSON payload: {data}")
â”‚        
â”‚                # Store the data in the database
â”‚                store_sensor_data(device_id, DeviceName, temperature, humidity, soil_moisture)
â”‚        
â”‚                # Determine action based on sensor data
â”‚                action = action_based_on_sensor(DeviceName, temperature, humidity, soil_moisture)
â”‚        
â”‚                response = {"DeviceName": DeviceName, "action": action}
â”‚                return jsonify(response)
â”‚        
â”‚            except Exception as e:
â”‚                print(f"Error processing request: {e}")
â”‚                return jsonify({"error": "Internal Server Error"}), 500
â”‚        â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘

â”‚        from flask import request, jsonify
â”‚        import time
â”‚        from sqlalchemy import desc
â”‚        from datetime import datetime
â”‚        from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
â”‚        from database_setup import (
â”‚            SessionLocal, SensorData, Sensor, Device, UserInteraction,
â”‚            Actuator, WeightedAverageFusionData, KalmanFilterFusionData
â”‚        )
â”‚        from weightedAverage import process_weighted_fusion
â”‚        
â”‚        # Authentication credentials for devices
â”‚        credentials = {
â”‚            "Ventilation_System_ESP": "password",
â”‚            "Irrigation_System_ESP": "password",
â”‚            "web_control": "web_password"
â”‚        }
â”‚        
â”‚        # Constants
â”‚        DEFAULT_USER_ID = 5000  # Server user
â”‚        TEMP_THRESHOLD = 30
â”‚        HUM_THRESHOLD = 40
â”‚        SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD = 30
â”‚        
â”‚        TEMP_SENSOR_IDS = [2099, 2092, 3093]
â”‚        HUM_SENSOR_IDS = [2091, 2034, 3027]
â”‚        WEIGHTS = [0.5, 0.3, 0.2]
â”‚        
â”‚        # Actuator Names
â”‚        INTAKE_SHUTTER = "intake_shutter"
â”‚        WATER_PUMP = "water_pump"
â”‚        VENTILATION_FAN = "ventilation_fan"
â”‚        
â”‚        # Device IDs
â”‚        Ventilation_System_ESP_ID = 2000
â”‚        Irrigation_System_ESP_ID = 3000
â”‚        
â”‚        soil_sensor_1id = 2005
â”‚        soil_sensor_2id = 3002
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚        def get_fused_values_by_sensors(session: Session, *sensor_ids: int):
â”‚            fused_values = {}
â”‚        
â”‚            if not sensor_ids:
â”‚                return fused_values  # No IDs provided â†’ return empty
â”‚        
â”‚            for sensor_id in sensor_ids:
â”‚                if sensor_id is None:
â”‚                    continue
â”‚                fusion = (
â”‚                    session.query(KalmanFilterFusionData)
â”‚                    .filter_by(SensorID=sensor_id)
â”‚                    .order_by(desc(KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp))
â”‚                    .first()
â”‚                )
â”‚                if fusion:
â”‚                    fused_values[sensor_id] = fusion.FusedValue
â”‚        
â”‚            return fused_values
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚        def log_user_action(session, device_id, action, user_id, actuator_id):
â”‚            session.add(UserInteraction(
â”‚                DeviceID=device_id,
â”‚                Action=action,
â”‚                UserID=user_id,
â”‚                ActuatorID=actuator_id,
â”‚                Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()
â”‚            ))
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚        def control_actuator(session, actuator_name, status, user_id):
â”‚            actuator = session.query(Actuator).filter_by(ActuatorName=actuator_name).first()
â”‚            if not actuator:
â”‚                actuator = Actuator(
â”‚                    ActuatorName=actuator_name,
â”‚                    Status=status,
â”‚                    LastUpdated=datetime.utcnow(),
â”‚                    UserID=user_id
â”‚                )
â”‚                session.add(actuator)
â”‚            else:
â”‚                if actuator.Status != status:
â”‚                    actuator.Status = status
â”‚                    actuator.LastUpdated = datetime.utcnow()
â”‚                    actuator.UserID = user_id
â”‚                    log_user_action(
â”‚                        session,
â”‚                        device_id=actuator.ActuatorID,
â”‚                        action=f"{actuator_name}_{status.lower()}",
â”‚                        user_id=user_id,
â”‚                        actuator_id=actuator.ActuatorID
â”‚                    )
â”‚            session.commit()
â”‚            return actuator
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚        def get_latest_fused_temperature_humidity(session):
â”‚            latest_temp = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData).filter_by(
â”‚                SensorType="temperature").order_by(desc(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp)).first()
â”‚            latest_hum = session.query(WeightedAverageFusionData).filter_by(
â”‚                SensorType="humidity").order_by(desc(WeightedAverageFusionData.Timestamp)).first()
â”‚        
â”‚            return {
â”‚                "temperature": latest_temp.FusedValue if latest_temp else None,
â”‚                "humidity": latest_hum.FusedValue if latest_hum else None
â”‚            }
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚        def action_based_on_sensor(user_id=DEFAULT_USER_ID):
â”‚            with SessionLocal() as session:
â”‚                result = get_fused_values_by_sensors(session, soil_sensor_1id, soil_sensor_2id)
â”‚                soil1 = result.get(soil_sensor_1id)
â”‚                soil2 = result.get(soil_sensor_2id)
â”‚        
â”‚                soil_moisture = None
â”‚                if soil1 is not None and soil2 is not None:
â”‚                    average = (soil1 + soil2) / 2
â”‚                    if 0 <= average <= 100:
â”‚                        soil_moisture = average
â”‚                elif soil1 is not None:
â”‚                    if 0 <= soil1 <= 100:
â”‚                        soil_moisture = soil1
â”‚                elif soil2 is not None:
â”‚                    if 0 <= soil2 <= 100:
â”‚                        soil_moisture = soil2
â”‚                # Else â†’ soil_moisture stays None
â”‚        
â”‚                temperature=process_weighted_fusion(sensor_ids=TEMP_SENSOR_IDS, weights=WEIGHTS, sensor_type="Temperature")
â”‚        
â”‚                # Call for humidity
â”‚                humidity=process_weighted_fusion(sensor_ids=HUM_SENSOR_IDS, weights=WEIGHTS, sensor_type="Humidity")
â”‚        
â”‚                actions = []
â”‚        
â”‚                try:
â”‚                    if temperature is not None and humidity is not None:
â”‚                        if temperature > TEMP_THRESHOLD or humidity > HUM_THRESHOLD:
â”‚                            control_actuator(session, VENTILATION_FAN, "on", user_id)
â”‚                            control_actuator(session, INTAKE_SHUTTER, "on", user_id)
â”‚                            actions.append("Ventilation_ON")
â”‚                        elif temperature < TEMP_THRESHOLD and humidity < HUM_THRESHOLD:
â”‚                            control_actuator(session, VENTILATION_FAN, "off", user_id)
â”‚                            control_actuator(session, INTAKE_SHUTTER, "off", user_id)
â”‚                            actions.append("Ventilation_OFF")
â”‚        
â”‚                    if soil_moisture is not None:
â”‚                        if soil_moisture < SOIL_MOISTURE_THRESHOLD:
â”‚                            control_actuator(session, WATER_PUMP, "on", user_id)
â”‚                            actions.append("Irrigation_ON")
â”‚                        else:
â”‚                            control_actuator(session, WATER_PUMP, "off", user_id)
â”‚                            actions.append("Irrigation_OFF")
â”‚        
â”‚                    session.commit()
â”‚                    return ", ".join(actions) if actions else "none"
â”‚                except Exception as e:
â”‚                    session.rollback()
â”‚                    print(f"[ERROR] Failed to perform action: {e}")
â”‚                    return "error"
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚        def get_or_create_device(session, device_id, device_name):
â”‚            device = session.query(Device).filter_by(DeviceID=device_id).first()
â”‚            if not device:
â”‚                device = Device(DeviceID=device_id, DeviceName=device_name, Location="Unknown", Status="Active")
â”‚                session.add(device)
â”‚                session.commit()
â”‚                session.refresh(device)
â”‚            return device
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚        def get_or_create_sensor(session,sensor_id, device_id, sensor_type):
â”‚            sensor = session.query(Sensor).filter_by(SensorID=sensor_id, SensorType=sensor_type).first()
â”‚            if not sensor:
â”‚                sensor = Sensor(SensorID=sensor_id, DeviceID=device_id, SensorType=sensor_type, Location="Unknown", Status="Active")
â”‚                session.add(sensor)
â”‚                session.commit()
â”‚                session.refresh(sensor)
â”‚            return sensor
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚        def store_sensor_value(session, sensor, value):
â”‚            session.add(SensorData(SensorID=sensor.SensorID, Value=value, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
â”‚        
â”‚        
â”‚        def store_sensor_data(device_id, device_name,sensor_id,
â”‚                              temperature=None, filtered_temperature=None,
â”‚                              humidity=None, filtered_humidity=None,
â”‚                              soil_moisture=None, filtered_soil_moisture=None):
â”‚            with SessionLocal() as session:
â”‚                try:
â”‚                    get_or_create_device(session, device_id, device_name)
â”‚        
â”‚                    if temperature is not None:
â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "temperature")
â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, temperature)
â”‚        
â”‚                    if filtered_temperature is not None:
â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "temperature_filtered")
â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, filtered_temperature)
â”‚        
â”‚                    if humidity is not None:
â”‚                        sensor = get_or_create_sensor(session, device_id, "humidity")
â”‚                        store_sensor_value(session, sensor, humidity)
â”‚        
â”‚                    if filtered_humidity is not None:

â”‚            interaction = UserInteraction(
â”‚                DeviceID=device_id,
â”‚                Action=action,
â”‚                UserID=user_id,
â”‚                Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()
â”‚            )

â”‚        def control_actuator(session, actuator_name, status, user_id):
â”‚            actuator = session.query(Actuator).filter_by(ActuatorName=actuator_name).first()
â”‚            if not actuator:
â”‚                actuator = Actuator(ActuatorName=actuator_name, Status=status, LastUpdated=datetime.utcnow(), UserID=user_id)
â”‚                session.add(actuator)
â”‚            else:
â”‚                actuator.Status = status
â”‚                actuator.LastUpdated = datetime.utcnow()
â”‚                actuator.UserID = user_id
â”‚        
â”‚            # Log who triggered this actuator
â”‚            log_user_action(session, device_id=actuator.ActuatorID, action=f"{actuator_name}_{status.lower()}", user_id=user_id)
â”‚            return True

â”‚                    action_taken = "Irrigation_System_on"

â”‚                session.rollback()
â”‚                print(f"[ERROR] Failed to perform action: {e}")
â”‚                return "error"

â”‚        def store_sensor_data(device_id, DeviceName, temperature=None, filtered_temperature=None, humidity=None, filtered_humidity=None, soil_moisture=None, filtered_soil_moisture= None):
â”‚            session = SessionLocal()

â”‚            try:
â”‚                # Ensure device exists
â”‚                device = session.query(Device).filter_by(DeviceID=device_id).first()
â”‚                if not device:
â”‚                    device = Device(DeviceID=device_id, DeviceName=DeviceName, Type="ESP32", Location="Unknown", Status="Active")
â”‚                    session.add(device)
â”‚                    session.commit()
â”‚                    session.refresh(device)
â”‚        
â”‚                # Store relevant sensor data
â”‚                if temperature is not None and device_id in {1, 2, 3, 4}:
â”‚                    session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="temperature", Value=temperature, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
â”‚                if filtered_temperature is not None and device_id in {1, 2, 3, 4}:
â”‚                    session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, FusedValue=temperature, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
â”‚                if humidity is not None and device_id in {5, 6, 7, 8}:
â”‚                    session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="humidity", Value=humidity, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
â”‚                if filtered_humidity is not None and device_id in {5, 6, 7, 8}:
â”‚                    session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, FusedValue=temperature, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
â”‚                if soil_moisture is not None and device_id in {9,10}:
â”‚                    session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, SensorType="soil_moisture", Value=soil_moisture, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
â”‚                if filtered_soil_moisture is not None and device_id in {9,10}:
â”‚                    session.add(SensorData(DeviceID=device_id, FusedValue=temperature, Timestamp=datetime.utcnow()))
â”‚                session.commit()
â”‚        
â”‚            except Exception as e:
â”‚                session.rollback()
â”‚                print(f"[ERROR] Failed to store sensor data: {e}")
â”‚            finally:
â”‚                session.close()

â”‚        
â”‚                process_weighted_fusion()

â”‚

â”‚                print(f"[ERROR] Exception in receive_sensor_data: {e}")
â”‚                return jsonify({"error": "Internal Server Error"}), 500

â””â”€â”€ weightedAverage.py
     â†“â†“â†“ FILE CONTENT â†“â†“â†“
     from datetime import datetime, timedelta
     from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     from database_setup import KalmanFilterFusionData, WeightedAverageFusionData, SessionLocal
     
     
     def weighted_average_fusion(values, weights):
         """Perform weighted average of given values with weights."""
         if len(values) != len(weights):
             raise ValueError("Length of values and weights must match.")
         return sum(v * w for v, w in zip(values, weights))
     
     
     def fetch_recent_sensor_data(session, sensor_ids, window_seconds):
         """Fetch the most recent Kalman-filtered readings for given sensor_ids within time window."""
         now = datetime.utcnow()
         window_start = now - timedelta(seconds=window_seconds)
         latest_data = {}
     
         for sensor_id in sensor_ids:
             entry = session.query(KalmanFilterFusionData)\
                 .filter(KalmanFilterFusionData.SensorID == sensor_id)\
                 .filter(KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp >= window_start)\
                 .order_by(KalmanFilterFusionData.Timestamp.desc())\
                 .first()
             if entry:
                 latest_data[sensor_id] = entry.FusedValue
     
         return latest_data
     
     
     def process_weighted_fusion(sensor_ids, weights, sensor_type, fusion_window_seconds=60):
         """
         Run weighted average fusion on a given set of sensor IDs and weights.
     
         Args:
             sensor_ids (list): List of sensor IDs.
             weights (list): Corresponding weights (same length as sensor_ids).
             sensor_type (str): Sensor type label (e.g., "Temperature", "Humidity").
             fusion_window_seconds (int): Time window in seconds to consider valid readings.
         """
         session: Session = SessionLocal()
         try:
             sensor_data = fetch_recent_sensor_data(session, sensor_ids, fusion_window_seconds)
     
             if not sensor_data:
                 print(f"[{sensor_type.upper()}] No recent readings available.")
                 return
     
             available_ids = list(sensor_data.keys())
             available_values = [sensor_data[sid] for sid in available_ids]
     
             # Adjust weights to match available sensors
             weight_map = {sid: w for sid, w in zip(sensor_ids, weights)}
             available_weights = [weight_map[sid] for sid in available_ids]
     
     
             # Normalize weights
             total_weight = sum(available_weights)
             normalized_weights = [w / total_weight for w in available_weights]
     
             fused_value = weighted_average_fusion(available_values, normalized_weights)
     
             session.add(WeightedAverageFusionData(
                 SensorType=sensor_type,
                 Timestamp=datetime.utcnow(),
                 FusedValue=fused_value
             ))
             session.commit()
             print(f"[{sensor_type.upper()}] Fused value: {fused_value:.2f} from {len(available_values)} sensors.")
         except Exception as e:
             session.rollback()
             print(f"[ERROR] Fusion failed for {sensor_type}: {e}")
         finally:
             session.close()
     â†‘â†‘â†‘ END OF FILE â†‘â†‘â†‘
